
-----title
新余 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a4201293d58c439da3de0716cf571b58_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a4201293d58c439da3de0716cf571b58");'><span id='a4201293d58c439da3de0716cf571b58_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1033')">1019-1033年</a>，1-15岁</div><div id='a4201293d58c439da3de0716cf571b58' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年</a>　是年，刘敞生，伯父刘立言中进士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1021')">1020-1021年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1022&endYear=1022')">1022年</a>　居乡，是年，父刘立之改太子中舍，自婺州金华县移梓州中江县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　居乡，弟攽生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>　居乡，弟刘攽所作《行状》称刘敞少年老成。叔父刘立礼中宋郊榜进士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1031')">1025-1031年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　居乡，父刘立之知高邮军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　居乡，习为古文。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f773d9e72dea47b49efafc5e8ff808b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f773d9e72dea47b49efafc5e8ff808b5");'><span id='f773d9e72dea47b49efafc5e8ff808b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1036')">1034-1036年</a>，16-18岁</div><div id='f773d9e72dea47b49efafc5e8ff808b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　父刘立之除福建路提点刑狱，敞随父入闽，识张宜，遂为忘年交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　已多有著述。作品：《疑礼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十六。）</span><div id='poem_1173824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>疑礼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173824")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173824'>今之《礼》非醇经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173824_comment'></div>周道衰，孔子没，圣人之徒合百说而杂编之，至汉而始备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173824_comment'></div>其间多六国秦汉之制，离文断句，统一不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173824_comment'></div>惟《曾子问》一篇最详，而又不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173824_comment'></div>其问曰：「君葬而世子生，则如之何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173824_comment'></div>对曰：「三月而告于祢」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173824_comment'></div>吾疑非仲尼之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173824_comment'></div>古者诸侯将薨，无世子，则命贵公子先为之定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173824_comment'></div>命之定，则后无篡夺之忧，虽愚人亦知其必然，又恶有既殡而待世子生乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173824_comment'></div>既殡而待且不可，况既葬而待乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173824_comment'></div>既葬而待，是或旷年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173824_comment'></div>《春秋》诸侯逾年无君，最其重也，况旷年乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173824_comment'></div>士三月无君则相吊，此士无君也，况果无君乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173824_comment'></div>苟以君之重嫡，不可不须焉，则夫人之生也不可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173824_comment'></div>苟为世子焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173824_comment'></div>苟为女子焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173824_comment'></div>如遂女子，亦将尊之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173824_comment'></div>或曰：「此谓世子生而告神之礼也，非须以为君也，为君者先定矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173824_comment'></div>此不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173824_comment'></div>其名之以世子，举之以继体之义，宰祝从之，有君仪焉，何谓非君？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173824_comment'></div>或曰：「其诸将反先定者而授之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173824_comment'></div>曰：「恶，是何言也，为人后者，为之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173824_comment'></div>彼既为后矣，屡易之可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173824_comment'></div>或曰：「吾闻之，参也鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173824_comment'></div>问之几是乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173824_comment'></div>曰：「问之者对之，固亦宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173824_comment'></div>鲁何独参也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173824_comment'></div>昔者《春秋》讥惠公不早分其嫡庶，以底大乱，又奚为此论哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173824_comment'></div>或曰：「三年之间，有冢宰焉，此其见之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173824_comment'></div>曰：「冢宰者奚设哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173824_comment'></div>设以佑嗣子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173824_comment'></div>设以待嗣子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173824_comment'></div>且冢宰亦何常之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173824_comment'></div>有伊尹之心则可，无则篡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173824_comment'></div>安能望人人于伊尹哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173824_comment'></div>其亦可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173824_comment'></div>予以谓质家亲亲先立弟，文家尊尊先立子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173824_comment'></div>圣人之意，必有从乎此，不在乎彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173824_comment'></div>且成王幼，周公以为忧，况日以冀、月以望乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173824_comment'></div>吾以是观之，今之《礼》非醇经，审矣！</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1173824_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　弟刘攽作[彩选格]，敞为之序。作品：《汉官仪》序。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='94d7d184bff54432a90f99b2ee4725f8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("94d7d184bff54432a90f99b2ee4725f8");'><span id='94d7d184bff54432a90f99b2ee4725f8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1038')">1037-1038年</a>，19-20岁</div><div id='94d7d184bff54432a90f99b2ee4725f8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　父刘立之转司勋员外郎，入朝，拜开封府判官，敞随父入朝，作《志雪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十四。）</span><div id='poem_1173877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>志雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173877")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173877'>闽越地滨海，气窳薄多旸，余三年居之，未始见雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173877_comment'></div>明年丁丑来京师，秋即雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173877_comment'></div>长老或以为寡，人知其寡，或共议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173877_comment'></div>或曰：「九月于卦为《剥》，《剥》五阴一阳，阴虽太盛，阳亦未绝，未当雨雪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173877_comment'></div>然雨雪者，阴太早，刑太急也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173877_comment'></div>或曰：「物不时为灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173877_comment'></div>雪当降于冬，不当降于秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173877_comment'></div>降于秋，不时也，是当为灾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173877_comment'></div>人解之曰：「否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173877_comment'></div>凡以卦为《剥》，阴虽盛，阳尚存，不当雪者，是十一月雪，亦可怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173877_comment'></div>十一月阳始生固微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173877_comment'></div>正月三阳而雪，人不怪也，何以独怪秋也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173877_comment'></div>且三阳为《泰》，《泰》时雨雪犹可，五阴为《剥》，《剥》时雨雪，何以不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173877_comment'></div>而谓之刑失乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173877_comment'></div>且刑何以失？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173877_comment'></div>夫古者昏乱之时，天子不隐愚，大夫不爱人，吏不哀矜，鳏寡不见收，则狱有过而气有变耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173877_comment'></div>今天子圣而明，大夫谨而详，吏畏而法，鳏寡悦而安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173877_comment'></div>其于刑也，讯从恕，议从厚，疑从赦，何致于失而雪哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173877_comment'></div>此议之非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173877_comment'></div>又凡所谓不时而灾者，谓害于岁耳，今九月雪，何以害也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173877_comment'></div>谷已入则不害，麦已布则不害，民已室处授衣则不害，鸟兽既氄则不害，昆虫已蛰则不害，而犹谓九月雪为不时，失类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173877_comment'></div>夫南方地卑故瘅暑，北方地高自倍，南方盛冬无雪非异，故北方未冬为雪何怪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173877_comment'></div>且雪不当降于秋，降于冬可也，降于春可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173877_comment'></div>夫春犹秋也，世不怪春雪，何怪秋雪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173877_comment'></div>人傥以少见为疑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173877_comment'></div>夫麦宿种而性能寒，故种麦而雪，殆丰年祥也，未可议」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173877_comment'></div>明年麦果大收，倍于昔年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173877_comment'></div>然则二者之言，前果谬，后大信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173877_comment'></div>人见所鲜，即议以为怪，为不时，为灾，则凡出处异于世，言语异于世，文采异于世，世所谓鲜而可怪者，以施于事，必以谓不时，行之于民，则以谓且有灾，然卒无灾有福者多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173877_comment'></div>世人岂但好论议哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173877_comment'></div>亦怪其非常、与己殊致耳，然则是与非未可信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173877_comment'></div>是岁也，秋复雪，明年吾又将贺民之丰麦也，故志焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1173877_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年12月</a>　十二月壬辰，知饶州范仲淹改知润州，有《闻范饶州移疾》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十一。）</span><div id='poem_498872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻范饶州移疾</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498872")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498872'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498872'>汲黯廉平汉主知，淮阳移病苦情羸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498872'>偃藩政事应无及，伏阁精神定未衰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498872'>天欲期人身必乏，帝疑飞将数多奇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498872'>何当半夜开宣室，独使雍容对受釐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498872'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498872_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　在京，作《不举贤良为非议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>不举贤良为非议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173841")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173841'>景祐四年，诏举贤良方正之士，至者数十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173841_comment'></div>明年，有司试其艺，独二人应科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173841_comment'></div>于是宰相议以贤良猥众，多名少实，欲一切罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173841_comment'></div>余在京师，作此议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173841_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1173841'>贤良通于古今之变，政教之本，岂止心辨善辞，以自鬻一时哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173841_comment'></div>今夫天子深居皋库之中，而洞视四海之广，虽有日月之明，不能隐于幡旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173841_comment'></div>故外有登闻、匦函，内有银台、閤门，而设御史、谏官，是纪是纲，则岂不欲尽下情而断欺负哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173841_comment'></div>虽然，民能自诣登闻、匦函者，非必有长材异画，动主听者也，特州里细故，诉困于上，不则利其身以禄者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173841_comment'></div>臣能自致银台、閤门者，非必有谠言切辞，为国忧者也，特簿书往来，各守一端，不则幸其遇以求位者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173841_comment'></div>夫细故不举，不足为天下忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173841_comment'></div>簿书不期会，不足为朝廷病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173841_comment'></div>由是而言，虽使百登闻、匦函，不若十贤良之尽下情也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173841_comment'></div>虽使十银台、閤门，不若一方正之识本务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173841_comment'></div>谏官、御史，位隆志满，充庭取备，不若使草野之士直言而极谏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173841_comment'></div>夫古之取士者，选之于乡，举之于民，三公宾而荐之，天子拜而受之，是以礼义全而廉让作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173841_comment'></div>其意盖曰贤能重而禄位轻云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173841_comment'></div>是以或藏而不肯仕，或走而不肯见，其意亦曰吾之身重于禄位云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173841_comment'></div>故君人者，趣于人，不闻趣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173841_comment'></div>今天下之仕必由进士，求进士者又不谨于礼，聚之如召役，校之如试技，意可则荐，不可则黜，故进士之名至卑也，进士之礼至薄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173841_comment'></div>进士之仕茍易也，上重其禄，下轻其身，故洁己高世之士不肯从也，深自托于贤良而发愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173841_comment'></div>今大夫之议，谓贤良无益，而学者顾多奔竞，而可废勿举焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173841_comment'></div>呜呼，曷为其然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173841_comment'></div>大夫固患其无益欤，谓进士者乃有益哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173841_comment'></div>固患其多奔竞欤，则胡不使公卿举之，而乃使其自进也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173841_comment'></div>夫自进者多，则忘以利为耻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173841_comment'></div>使待举而动，而天下之人莫不以礼自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173841_comment'></div>如是而患奔竞者多，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173841_comment'></div>抑又有甚便者一焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173841_comment'></div>今公卿皆禄位自广，才德自高，耻有迎师之名，羞有廉士之问，其来长矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173841_comment'></div>今一旦敕之，使为国荐贤，宜人人用心，而天子必有垂拱无为之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173841_comment'></div>吾又以阅公卿之才，忠信者进，私党者退，譬若著之权衡，不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173841_comment'></div>使上无文仲窃位之过，下无伯尊攘善之祸，不亦大哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173841_comment'></div>所谓甚便者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173841_comment'></div>然则言贤良可废，非贤良之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173841_comment'></div>凡吏待之不以礼，使之不自重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173841_comment'></div>故礼之不谨，则贤者不出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173841_comment'></div>待之不厚，则贤者不劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173841_comment'></div>其理然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173841_comment'></div>又曷为废其举哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173841_comment'></div>天下洁己高俗之士焉所而发愤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1173841_comment'></div>忧国济世之士焉所而布策？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1173841_comment'></div>怀义愿忠之士焉所而赴诉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1173841_comment'></div>贪进苟得之士焉所而矫厉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1173841_comment'></div>且夫贤良，美称也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1173841_comment'></div>方正，善行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1173841_comment'></div>方为天下，而自不举贤良始，是使今之天下不得与周汉比隆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1173841_comment'></div>古之治国家者，有益于用则存之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1173841_comment'></div>夏后之鼎，汤之典宝，周之琬琰，鲁之大弓，晋之阙巩，卫之大吕，陈之石砮，和之弓，垂之矢，离之磬，胤之舞衣，此其非有通古今之变，明王道之本，达下情之塞，然而世掌之，况在其求人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1173841_comment'></div>故子贡欲去告朔之饩羊，仲尼不悦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1173841_comment'></div>臧文仲废六关，君子讥其不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1173841_comment'></div>然则循名而忘其实，失所以废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1173841_comment'></div>弃大而恤其小，失所以置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1173841_comment'></div>患不使有司举贤良，不患贤良无益也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1173841_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dfd5142054094129a922bfed79c2177e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dfd5142054094129a922bfed79c2177e");'><span id='dfd5142054094129a922bfed79c2177e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1046')">1045-1046年</a>，27-28岁</div><div id='dfd5142054094129a922bfed79c2177e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　在京，父刘立之复拜司勋员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　在京，作《送梅圣俞序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十五。）</span><div id='poem_1173761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送梅圣俞序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173761")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173761'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173761'>昔者边鄙无事，士大夫耻言兵，圣俞独先注《孙子》十三篇献之，可谓知权矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173761_comment'></div>及其有事，士大夫争言兵，或因以取富贵，圣俞更闭匿不省利害，可谓知道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173761_comment'></div>夫圣俞前非勇也，知天下忘战之必有忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173761_comment'></div>后非怯也，知功名之说胜则隳教化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173761_comment'></div>圣俞之任其身不轻矣，世人其若圣俞何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173761_comment'></div>某少圣俞十六岁，然圣俞与我为友，所以从之游，常恐不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173761_comment'></div>今圣俞应聘许昌，某以事留京师，不得偕行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173761_comment'></div>古者赠人以言，吾何以赠子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173761_comment'></div>明子之趣，以示人不欺耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173761_comment'></div>呜呼，世有君子者，以我为知言矣，于圣俞无负焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1173761_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　三月御试，与弟刘攽同中贾黯榜进士，授大理评事，通判蔡州事，时吴育为守。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　作《御试戎祀国之大事赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1173519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御试戎祀国之大事赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173519")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173519'>戎在御侮，祀专飨神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173519_comment'></div>皆有邦之大事，岂庶政以同伦？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173519_comment'></div>宜社而行，外伸威于殊俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173519_comment'></div>受釐以报，内均福于生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173519_comment'></div>盖所谓朝廷之先务，教化之本因者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173519_comment'></div>稽合前经，发挥至理，政有常法，事或殊轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173519_comment'></div>以保民者莫若戎，以驭神者莫如祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173519_comment'></div>善师不战，谅治体之孰加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173519_comment'></div>精意克禋，眷彝伦之莫拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173519_comment'></div>是故将命武事也，必有归脤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173519_comment'></div>将格神贶也，必先执膰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173519_comment'></div>盖大其所当大，尊其所可尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173519_comment'></div>干戈省躬，信丕经之斯在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173519_comment'></div>玉帛荐德，微末节以同论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173519_comment'></div>然则治道有后先，国务有小大，威四海者兵为急，叙五经者祭为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173519_comment'></div>民神之事不一，皆以底和平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173519_comment'></div>腥熟之俎不同，皆以福中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173519_comment'></div>故圣王劳意于用众，致诚于逆禧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173519_comment'></div>动则谨尔，下皆仰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173519_comment'></div>知夫事之大不在于彼，礼之重莫先于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173519_comment'></div>亦犹仲尼陈三慎之端，惟斋及战；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173519_comment'></div>箕子序八政之目，兼祀与师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173519_comment'></div>用能祭典不奸，天威无陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173519_comment'></div>或谨以进胙，或重之受脤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173519_comment'></div>迩遐一体，𢥠武节而服从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173519_comment'></div>上下交欢，欣德馨之明允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173519_comment'></div>故曰圣人之祭，不能独丰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173519_comment'></div>天下虽治，亦将御戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173519_comment'></div>大而慎之则蒙福，细而慢之则亡功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173519_comment'></div>谨禁暴戢兵之机，惟政之本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173519_comment'></div>明昭孝息民之义，何治之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173519_comment'></div>盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173519_comment'></div>丕冒群生，钦崇大节，非戎无以威远，非祀无以著洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173519_comment'></div>故蛮夷服而鬼神飨焉，有以缉熙于鸿烈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1173519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　为俞献卿作墓志铭。作品：《大中大夫行刑部侍郎致仕上柱国赐紫金鱼袋俞公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大中大夫行刑部侍郎致仕上柱国赐紫金鱼袋俞公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173929")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173929'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173929'>公讳献卿，字谏臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173929_comment'></div>其先河间人，晋永嘉之乱，徙居黟歙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173929_comment'></div>公之父曰某，赠工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173929_comment'></div>尚书之父曰某，某之父曰某，皆蓄德不仕，庆诒其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173929_comment'></div>尚书取闵氏，赠太原郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173929_comment'></div>实生二子，长曰献可，官至某官、天章閤待制，其季则公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173929_comment'></div>公之初学，师友其兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173929_comment'></div>强力敏捷，儒术自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173929_comment'></div>其后遂相续成进士，名闻天下云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173929_comment'></div>拜寿州芍陂尉，临事明察，善钩人情，推显至于隐，故盗贼不敢发，发又辄得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173929_comment'></div>人有告其师浮屠出游者，公揣其有奸，使吏拘之，而索其室，得浮屠之尸，一县大惊，以为有神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173929_comment'></div>转昭州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173929_comment'></div>陈进乱岭南，象州危甚，吏民莫自坚，其太守欲背城奔，使公往护之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173929_comment'></div>公至，为说利害，复教使坚壁治兵，为不可攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173929_comment'></div>太守急，听其言，得免诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173929_comment'></div>贼亦不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173929_comment'></div>官兵之在宣州，公部昭民往输之粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173929_comment'></div>及事平，议留昭民，伐山林以治官府，曰：「役病矣，不可以不示信」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173929_comment'></div>请期三日，许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173929_comment'></div>民闻公令，知不久役，皆劝功趣事，事如其素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173929_comment'></div>陈进死，上功第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173929_comment'></div>赏未行，丁尚书忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173929_comment'></div>丧毕，转大理寺丞，为本寺详断官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173929_comment'></div>选殿中丞，知庐州慎县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173929_comment'></div>又换杭州仁和县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173929_comment'></div>丁母夫人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173929_comment'></div>服除，改太常博士，知南雄州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173929_comment'></div>潮阳吏民不相能，讼系不决，一郡恟恟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173929_comment'></div>徙公知潮阳，镌其曲直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173929_comment'></div>潮阳又多水害，公亲相地势，筑防金山，百姓便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173929_comment'></div>转屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173929_comment'></div>大臣荐可为执法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173929_comment'></div>历两院御史，领左军巡使，举察称职，拜三司盐铁判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173929_comment'></div>上初即位，公疏言：「民力不足，其弊在取之太繁，用之太奢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173929_comment'></div>可减冗食及诸无益，引先帝为法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173929_comment'></div>累数百言，天子嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173929_comment'></div>罢清卫兵及省浮屠老子祠醮，公本谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173929_comment'></div>淮南、二浙，一岁耗盐十三万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173929_comment'></div>尚书经费不足，公往视之，至则条废旧弊，以新法从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173929_comment'></div>吏尽偿所负，又增五百万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1173929_comment'></div>以兄为盐铁副使，改开封府推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1173929_comment'></div>会陕西言兵食不足，转运使非其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1173929_comment'></div>朝议换之，上亦重其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1173929_comment'></div>宰相数奏进拟，无合意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1173929_comment'></div>召公问状，公不辞让，因入言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1173929_comment'></div>天子识公名，曰：「是前使淮南者，可奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1173929_comment'></div>公至部三日，得半年之储，终岁馀二年之食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1173929_comment'></div>虽一切方略，然其百姓富者不病，贫者不扰云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1173929_comment'></div>泾原塞外武延川，本羌地，诸将欲改名，请筑堡凿濠守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1173929_comment'></div>公奏以谓生事，不可许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1173929_comment'></div>已而寇果至，杀掠吏士，塞所凿濠而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1173929_comment'></div>转兵部员外郎，迁京西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1173929_comment'></div>召对边事，荐赵某可将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1173929_comment'></div>赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1173929_comment'></div>以兄没当葬，求为东南官，改福建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1173929_comment'></div>召还，判盐铁勾院，转刑部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1173929_comment'></div>居二年，命直史馆、知荆南府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1173929_comment'></div>进见言事，上听不倦，喜曰：「卿不当往荆州」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1173929_comment'></div>即日拜三司户部副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1173929_comment'></div>历度支盐铁三部，转右谏议大夫，复出荆南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1173929_comment'></div>满岁授直集贤学士、知杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1173929_comment'></div>登石作堤，以捍江涛，水不为灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1173929_comment'></div>召回，判三班院及银台、门下省，出为宣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1173929_comment'></div>元昊畔，西边大扰，诏书问所欲施，公条上十馀事，朝廷称其知时务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1173929_comment'></div>徙知应天府，改工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1173929_comment'></div>以疾请老，天子忧之，以为刑部侍郎致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1173929_comment'></div>闻其居杭州，即从徙二子官吴中，以便奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1173929_comment'></div>庆历五年四月十七日终于所居，享年七十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1173929_comment'></div>明年某月某日葬歙州某县之某原，从先人居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1173929_comment'></div>夫人冯翊郡君钱氏，柔淑知礼，是配是宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1173929_comment'></div>子四人：长希楚，某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1173929_comment'></div>次希元，进士及第，早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1173929_comment'></div>次希及，次希忠，皆将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1173929_comment'></div>女三人：长适秘书丞江杞，其二未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1173929_comment'></div>公为人高明刚严，论议立规矩，似不能容物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1173929_comment'></div>至典法持狱，平易宽恕，不肯妄有轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1173929_comment'></div>其在京西，钱丞相为许州，厚宾客之奉，岁费千万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1173929_comment'></div>执政素不说，又疑其有私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1173929_comment'></div>公奏事至京师，开其端问公，公对曰：「无他」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1173929_comment'></div>世称公长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1173929_comment'></div>累阶至大中大夫，勋至上柱国，爵至开国伯，食邑至九百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1173929_comment'></div>所与交游同僚，多历两府事，而公独不遂，可谓命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1173929_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_1173929'>俞之先世，基德相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1173929_comment'></div>其大而章，自公兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1173929_comment'></div>雍雍在家，矫矫在官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1173929_comment'></div>历试以难，富贵不愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1173929_comment'></div>忠而好谋，天子是咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1173929_comment'></div>功济西方，国人不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1173929_comment'></div>辞老而休，亦不踰矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1173929_comment'></div>其风孔高，以惮进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1173929_comment'></div>仲尼有言，积善馀庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1173929_comment'></div>公实有子，嗣武其盛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_91_1173929_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c133f4e2a3e9485a9d10fdaad2ac73df_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c133f4e2a3e9485a9d10fdaad2ac73df");'><span id='c133f4e2a3e9485a9d10fdaad2ac73df_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1055')">1051-1055年</a>，33-37岁</div><div id='c133f4e2a3e9485a9d10fdaad2ac73df' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年2月</a>　二月，服除，还为大理评事，召试学士院，擢太子中允、直集贤院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年9月</a>　九月，上《论修商胡口疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论修商胡口疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173583")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173583'>臣闻天有时，地有势，民有力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173583_comment'></div>圣王之建功谋事者，不与天分时，不与地分势，不与民分力，则功成而事立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173583_comment'></div>今朝廷以河决商胡，议必塞之，臣窃谓过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173583_comment'></div>乃者霖雨淫溢，山谷发泄，经川横溃，或冲冒城郭，此天时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173583_comment'></div>澶、魏之埽，如商胡者多矣，咸决而商胡独败，此地势也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173583_comment'></div>淮、汝以西，关陕以东，数千里之间，罹于水忧者，甚则溺死，不甚则流亡，夫妇愁痛，无所控告，略计百万人，未闻朝廷有以振业之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173583_comment'></div>而议塞河，强疲病之馀以极其力，乘残耗之后以略其财，重为事而罚所不胜，急为期而诛所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173583_comment'></div>上则与天争时，下则与地争势，此臣所谓过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173583_comment'></div>臣闻河之为患于中国久矣，其在前代，或塞或不塞，今塞之为仁，不塞不为不仁，此有时而否者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173583_comment'></div>以尧为君，以舜为臣，以禹为司空，十有三年，而后仅能胜水患耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173583_comment'></div>今朝廷之无禹明矣，而欲以数月之间塞决河，不权于时，不察于民，不亦甚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173583_comment'></div>议者以为，不塞河则冀州之水可哀，甚不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173583_comment'></div>夫河未决之时，能使水不病冀州则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173583_comment'></div>既决之后，县邑则已没矣，人民则已亡矣，府库则已丧矣，虽塞河不能有救也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173583_comment'></div>今且纵水之所欲往而利导之，其不能救与彼同，而可以息民，何嫌而不为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173583_comment'></div>《诗》云：「民亦劳止，汔可小康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173583_comment'></div>惠此中国，以绥四方」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173583_comment'></div>夫中国者，固四方之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173583_comment'></div>惟陛下与知道者虑之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1173583_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年10月</a>　十月上《乞阔略唐介之罪书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷。）</span><div id='poem_1173598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞阔略唐介之罪疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173598")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173598'>臣伏闻陛下以殿中侍御史里行唐介言事狂狷，责授春州别驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173598_comment'></div>寻又闻陛下以春州险远，瘴疠之地，怜其孤危，将不生全，改授英州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173598_comment'></div>此诚陛下圣德厚恩，容忍臣子，万万无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173598_comment'></div>臣窃观《诗》、《书》所载，帝王之君，德莫盛于知过，仁莫大于好生，名莫荣于听谏，陛下皆践之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173598_comment'></div>且唐介居下讪上，至陷于戾，而陛下察其本心，以忠信为之，故曰「知过」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173598_comment'></div>既责介身，投之远方，而复忧其不全，故曰「好生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173598_comment'></div>当介初得罪之时，中外震动，以言为戒，及闻徙还英州，人人忻幸，知陛下无意杀之，忠义者更思竭尽，故曰「听谏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173598_comment'></div>臣不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173598_comment'></div>闻伊尹戒商王曰：「有言逆于汝心，必求诸道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173598_comment'></div>有言逊于汝志，必求诸非道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173598_comment'></div>此商所以保乂四海，格于皇天者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173598_comment'></div>臣窃谓介之所言虽逆耳，求之于道，亦当有合者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173598_comment'></div>陛下幸宽全不诛矣，若复阔略其罪，优游其身，俾得省过追咎，复齿朝列，于以开广言路，劝来者，则盛德无疆，高视上古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173598_comment'></div>臣不胜犬马之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1173598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年12月</a>　十二月，为陈耿作墓志铭。作品：《朝散大夫殿中丞知汝州叶县骑都尉陈君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫殿中丞知汝州叶县骑都尉陈君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173933")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173933'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173933'>君讳耿，字仲操，真定人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173933_comment'></div>祖曰审交，父曰昌业，世世传郑氏《礼》，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173933_comment'></div>君受学父祖，祥符初，以经中第，得上元尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173933_comment'></div>历永定军司理参军、霸州录事参军、甘泉令，迁建雄军节度推官，知永济县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173933_comment'></div>丞相沂公镇魏，善其政，奏徙大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173933_comment'></div>大名治城内，事尤剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173933_comment'></div>岁满课最，得见上，拜权永清军节度判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173933_comment'></div>初，丞相率其属连奏，举君可京官，期必得之，而才稍迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173933_comment'></div>丞相以为赏薄，知其有亲，更敕其弟子融，辟君监光州茶场，便奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173933_comment'></div>数月，以忧免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173933_comment'></div>其后服除，为苏州观察支使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173933_comment'></div>达官钜人荐君材能于朝者，前后十馀章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173933_comment'></div>改秘书省著作佐郎、知霍丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173933_comment'></div>顷之移阆中，迁太子左赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173933_comment'></div>代还，除叶县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173933_comment'></div>未行，又迁殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173933_comment'></div>庆历八年十一月五日卒于家，享年七十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173933_comment'></div>君为人廉直，不阿势附俗，而内恕有爱，故长于为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173933_comment'></div>其在永定军，人有杀死于路者，贼不得，其子疑怨家所为，诣吏辨诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173933_comment'></div>吏以子言名捕诉者，按之，證逮詾詾，囚无以自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173933_comment'></div>君察其不真，讼系待讯，而急白守丞，请捕贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173933_comment'></div>守丞怒曰：「司理侮法耶，何敢为死罪解脱」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173933_comment'></div>遣他掾与司理杂治囚，笞掠数百千，囚不胜痛，诬服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173933_comment'></div>具狱待报，君犹守之不听，人皆为君惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173933_comment'></div>明年，博野县捕得真杀人者，举郡大惊，众乃皆伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173933_comment'></div>及为永济县，当契丹使往来道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173933_comment'></div>自先帝与戎约和结兄弟，岁时聘问，一以敌国礼待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173933_comment'></div>使者入境，天子使中贵人候迓馈劳，冠盖相属，其有求市，令所司调与之，以见中国广大，厚其欢心，而少从旁县赋取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173933_comment'></div>蹴迫令长，稽缓不如意，辄劾以违制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173933_comment'></div>文移仓猝，百姓骚扰，岁岁苦之，略比军兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173933_comment'></div>而县吏乡典亦利得其势，侵渔细民，其敝盖久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173933_comment'></div>及君至，为设方略，饮食供张百物，皆豫储待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173933_comment'></div>后使者过县，有所调取，不复及民，民便安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173933_comment'></div>王丞相由此知君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173933_comment'></div>其始至阆中，岁大旱，郡守希转运使意，不听民诉灾，民遮君自言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173933_comment'></div>君即诣府请之，犹不许，因趋出，悉取民所诉状属吏，以令蠲其租，而公文上转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173933_comment'></div>转运使初不悦，后无如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173933_comment'></div>文丞相守成都，闻而嘉之，更分遣官属，行视两川郡县之被灾者，皆奏除其租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173933_comment'></div>独阆中，由君免于流亡，而上恩浸淫，至于东西川十有馀万户矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173933_comment'></div>君晚升朝，赠其父大理寺丞，母崔氏仙游县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1173933_comment'></div>位虽不大显，世守荣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1173933_comment'></div>娶薛氏，封高平县君，先君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1173933_comment'></div>子五人，女四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1173933_comment'></div>初，君仕官过汝阴，乐之，筑室焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1173933_comment'></div>君既没三岁，十二月丙申，诸子裔奇、京、苏等，乃以君及高平之丧，葬怀音乡之高原，以成君志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1173933_comment'></div>奇举进士，与予同岁，孝友慈祥，予甚知之，故予得铭其葬，庶几不朽云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1173933_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1173933'>学如其才，有以显亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1173933_comment'></div>仕如其职，有以便民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1173933_comment'></div>寿尔厥年，夫又何怨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1173933_comment'></div>卜处于此，实惟君存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1173933_comment'></div>盖古别子，百世不迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1173933_comment'></div>尚越其延，施于后昆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1173933_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年12月</a>　十二月，与韩维游会灵观，各有赋诗。作品：诗题失考。<span class='inlineComment2'>（仁宗嘉祐三年十二月有《辛卯十二月同持国游会灵观各曾赋诗后一年会灵烧高下俱尽天子为先朝所为不忍废复治集禧略放渭阳帝祠制度五岳同宇毋乏事而已不能如向之钜丽也戊戌十二月以事过谒祠下作七言寄持国》诗，据其可知本年曾与韩维同游会灵观。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年12月</a>　作《秦昭和钟赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷一。《秦昭和钟赋》题[直集贤院作],姑附此。）</span><div id='poem_1173502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦昭和钟赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173502")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173502'>秘阁有秦昭和钟，形制绝异，其始得之豳、雍之间，其铭首曰「不显朕皇祖十有二公」云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173502_comment'></div>其藏于册府久矣，予因为之赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（直集贤院作。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173502_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1173502'>阅故府之藏器，历先秦之遗踪，哀三代之逾远，美昭和之宝钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173502_comment'></div>何形制之瑰谲，骇观听之鲜同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173502_comment'></div>上盘拿而夭矫，若腾蛟兮升龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173502_comment'></div>下纷结而扶倚，状菱华与芙蓉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173502_comment'></div>彼僻陋之小国，曾铸作之绝工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173502_comment'></div>非以其铭祖考之休烈，交人神之肃雍者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173502_comment'></div>越千祀而独存兮，俟有道而一见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173502_comment'></div>谅鬼神之图佑兮，谌盛德之幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173502_comment'></div>夫固夏声之所出兮，袭二周之馀徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173502_comment'></div>茍延陵之既没兮，哀知音其为谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173502_comment'></div>询款识之尚传兮，邈沮、颉之遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173502_comment'></div>世行隶之趋俗兮，又虽久而不觌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173502_comment'></div>响沈潜以寂默兮，文幽晦而蔽匿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173502_comment'></div>鲜人情之好假兮，在独异而为谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173502_comment'></div>幸蒙君之厚德兮，发阴壤之秘封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173502_comment'></div>去瓦石之污处兮，历君门之九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173502_comment'></div>庇高阁之虚爽兮，参众宝而见容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173502_comment'></div>俪笙镛以干际兮，终诡时而不逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173502_comment'></div>审则而仪量兮，尚毋惑于权度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173502_comment'></div>推律而考钧兮，犹将谨夫《韶》、《韶》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173502_comment'></div>等弃之而勿庸兮，喟观者之未悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173502_comment'></div>保厥美以安处兮，焉惆怅而怀遇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1173502_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　作《送和弟通判陕府》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十一。《送和弟通判陕府》，自注[余与和今年皆三十余岁]，姑附此。）</span><div id='poem_498675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送和弟通判陜府</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498675")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498675'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498675'>丹绂双纹绶，朱轓左画轮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498675'>平生固自负，归去亦荣亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498675'>美俗馀分陜，悲歌激在陈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498675'>别离俱未易，因目二毛新<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498675'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498675'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_498675_0'>⑴ 自注：予（原作子，据四库本改）与和今年皆三十馀岁。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498675_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　同判登闻鼓院，改判吏部南曹，三上疏论夏竦谥，仁宗纳之，改夏竦谥[文正]为[文庄]<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　作《三日同景仁邻几济川晦叔景口吕秘校刘判官会南曹饮五君皆尚书外郎刘吕修唐书官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷十二。诗有[秋气迎节至]句，自注[立秋前一日]，年谱系于此年。诗题中诸人除范镇、江休复、吕公著以外其余人姓名不详。）</span><div id='poem_498153' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498153' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498153?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三日同景仁邻几济川晦叔景□吕秘校刘判官会南曹饮五君皆尚书外郎刘吕修唐书官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498153")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498153_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498153'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498153'>秋气迎节至<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：立秋前一日。）</span>，凉雨乘高风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498153'>车马散北阙，冠盖会南宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498153'>从吏殆成隐，玩岁复将穷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498153'>簿书幸无他，谈笑偶多同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498153'>郎选冠一时，史才映群公。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498153'>著书骇深妙，闻道惴颛蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498153'>但愿窃馀论，常此樽不空。<div id='poem_sentence_6_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_498153'>寄迹三署老，不惭颜与冯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_498153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_498153'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_498153_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年8月</a>　八月，权判三司开拆司，仍兼南曹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年9月</a>　九月，侬智高叛乱，枢密副使狄青宣抚，就应否置副使，上仁宗《论狄青宣抚当置副使疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论狄青宣抚当置副使疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173599")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173599'>臣闻朝廷以狄青宣抚荆湖，经制盗贼，而议不置副，臣以为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173599_comment'></div>或曰置副而使中人为之，臣又以为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173599_comment'></div>臣闻上古王者之遣使命将也，必为之设介贰参佐，非独司纪纲，广谋策而已，亦以谨大事，备不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173599_comment'></div>今拥数万人之众，连四路之师，节制万里，吉凶所系，而单车临之，孤拱独立，猝有疾病不意之虞，无所仗托，莫相维持，非计之得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173599_comment'></div>狄青起于行伍而迁枢近，天下诚未见其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173599_comment'></div>方以盗贼之急，拥兵而出，故人人相望风采，愿闻成功，以得贞固干略之臣，参职共事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173599_comment'></div>设以中人为之，必大失事望，足以示陋，非朝廷之光也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173599_comment'></div>臣故曰：议不置副，不便；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173599_comment'></div>置副而使中人为之，亦不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173599_comment'></div>此臣所以拳拳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173599_comment'></div>盖先事而言者，常若迂阔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173599_comment'></div>后事而言者，常若不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173599_comment'></div>惟陛下留意刍尧，谨重军旅之任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1173599_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　上仁宗《论城古渭州有四不可疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论城古渭州有四不可疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173605")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173605'>臣今月二十二日奏公事，臣得预上殿，亲闻德音，以谓古渭州存之则为害，弃之则伤威，两者未决，询及左右，指音恳恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173605_comment'></div>臣诚独美陛下聪明谦逊，好谋无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173605_comment'></div>臣虽不闻公卿之议，然臣之愚，以为弃之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173605_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173605_comment'></div>朝廷与羌戎约和久矣，今一旦夺其地而城之，弃明信，规小利，使夷狄有以窥中国，不可一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173605_comment'></div>羌戎种落非一族也，自见稍侵，必人人怀疑，交谋间谍，以新城为比，或能相率大为边患，不可二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173605_comment'></div>自始筑城，到今半年耳，所费已钜万计，秦州为空竭，而调终馈运，不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173605_comment'></div>设复屯兵守之，日引月长，财尽力竭，则关中皆可忧，不可三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173605_comment'></div>向者虏出争利，多杀官军数千人，后虽击破其众，足以相当，而虏怨益深，其志复得故地而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173605_comment'></div>兵若不解，忧患方起，不可四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173605_comment'></div>假令新城足以蔽秦州，长无羌胡之虞，虽倾国守之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173605_comment'></div>不然，地形便利，贼能乘之，以窥边圉，虽倾国争之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173605_comment'></div>今失所重轻，而糜国财用，困民力，损士卒之命，以贪此咫尺之地，计功则可辱，言利则可耻，虑患则可忧，昭昭甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173605_comment'></div>而谈者不忍决之，谓为伤威，臣所不谕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173605_comment'></div>昔者舜伐三苗，三苗不服，益赞于禹，班师振旅，而有苗来格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173605_comment'></div>由此观之，帝王之威，在使物畏之，不在使物恶之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173605_comment'></div>故动以义，顺于理，则物畏之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173605_comment'></div>动以利，逆于理，则物恶之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173605_comment'></div>畏之则服，恶之则侮，自然之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173605_comment'></div>武帝黜丞相御史之请，而止不田车师、轮台，则天下复平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173605_comment'></div>元帝用贾捐之之策，而罢珠崖，则中国复安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173605_comment'></div>故以德言之，则不过舜禹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173605_comment'></div>以强言之，则不过汉武帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173605_comment'></div>以驭夷狄也，患枉于义，不患力不足也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173605_comment'></div>患逆于理，不患威之捐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173605_comment'></div>惟陛下察于此两者，以观利害之熟在，谋之贵多，断之贵独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173605_comment'></div>明鉴所以见容，古事所以知今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173605_comment'></div>臣不胜狂直之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1173605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　上《论天久不雨疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论天久不雨疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173584")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173584'>臣伏以古今之通义，主逸而臣劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173584_comment'></div>陛下亲听万几，日昃不倦，与群臣等勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173584_comment'></div>今又闻以天久不雨之故，降服彻膳，躬自暴露，夜辄升坛祷祠，达旦不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173584_comment'></div>此则圣躬之劳，过于群臣，群臣实未有及陛下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173584_comment'></div>臣窃闻之，不胜其忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173584_comment'></div>且水旱之数，未可前测，设复弥月连旬，不如圣意，陛下何能专以万乘之体，为群臣代劳哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173584_comment'></div>如令万一冒风寒霜露之苦，有所不怡，陛下当使谁受其责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173584_comment'></div>而宗庙社稷之忧，独在陛下，陛下不可不自爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173584_comment'></div>诗书百家、圣贤精论，皆曰：人者天地之心，人和则天地之和致矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173584_comment'></div>近者大赦，恩及四海，解宿逋，裁减常税，宥过除罪，与之自新，德厚如此，和气宜应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173584_comment'></div>而愆亢尤甚者，臣之愚，窃意今日政事，所褒进，所刑罚，所施舍，所废置，犹有未合人心，不当天意者，故令阴阳否隔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173584_comment'></div>陛下诚少加圣恩，延问正直，日新其德，则和气可致，时雨可望，何必降服彻膳，躬自暴露，涉风寒霜露之险，增宗庙社稷之忧，非计之安者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173584_comment'></div>陛下视群臣百姓如子，群臣百姓望陛下如父，父以子将失所之故，深自克责，不避灾疾，而子方宴然自若，不可谓孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173584_comment'></div>臣虽贱，窃不胜犬马之心，又以谓救旱之术，在彼不在此，故敢冒昧陈闻，惟陛下裁择<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173584_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1173584'>「久」上原衍「下」，据《国朝诸臣奏议》删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1173584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1173584'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_1173584_0'>⑴ 《公是集》卷三一。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷四○，《历代名臣奏议》卷三○○，《右编》卷五。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1173584_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　作《张忠定谥议》，其首句为[太常礼院谥故礼部尚书张公曰忠定，太子中允、直集贤院，同判吏部尚书南曹刘敞覆议]，故附于此。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张忠定谥议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173842")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173842'>太常礼院谥故礼部尚书张公曰忠定，太子中允、直集贤院、同判吏部尚书曹刘敞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1173842", 1173842, "Clauses/1/Comments/2")'>覆议</span>曰：尚书布衣之时，任侠自喜，破产以奉宾客，而借躯报仇，往往<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1173842", 1173842, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>过直</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173842_comment'></div>及读书为文，折节受学，则爽厉明白，务求道真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173842_comment'></div>至于策名试吏，俶傥奋发，思自见于世，不令己失时，盖有古贤之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173842_comment'></div>而神宗圣考，知人善任，使每尽其用，虽专断于外，而上不疑，此其所以感激慷慨，能成功名者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173842_comment'></div>夫英伟卓荦之人，固自负其材，可以意气忠信结，而不可以禄位富利取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173842_comment'></div>尚书再在蜀及他临莅，皆朝廷所倚重，或兵荒之馀，而言听计从，德泽下流，民到于今称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173842_comment'></div>盖君之图任一，则士之报施重，不其然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173842_comment'></div>自宋兴以来且百年，言治者甚众，其直己以事上，尽心以抚下，生有荣名，死有遗爱者，尚书殆无与并焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173842_comment'></div>末年以疾，害于朝谒，不至大位，士君子以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173842_comment'></div>今皇上甄德念功，使有司追赐之谥，而曰廉方公正，安民大虑，窃以谓无间然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173842_comment'></div>请从博士之论，以充太史之录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173842_comment'></div>谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1173842_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　是年，前夫人伦氏卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年4月</a>　迁权三司度支判官，始解南曹，赐绯衣银鱼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　作《救日论》三篇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十九。）</span><div id='poem_1173798' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173798' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173798?labeling=true' target='_blank'>救日论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173798")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173798_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173798'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173798'>《春秋左氏传》曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1173798", 1173798, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>二至</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1173798", 1173798, "Clauses/1/Comments/2")'>二分</span>，日有食之，不为灾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173798_comment'></div>又曰：「非正阳之月不鼓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173798_comment'></div>臣以为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173798_comment'></div>夫圣王所甚畏而事者莫如天，天神之最著而明者莫如日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173798_comment'></div>日者众阳之宗，人君之表也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173798_comment'></div>日有食之，天子则伐鼓于社，诸侯则伐鼓于朝，非为慕迂阔而涂民耳目也，明其阴侵阳，柔乘刚，臣蔽君，妻陵夫，逆德之渐，不可长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173798_comment'></div>如是则奚救奚不救？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173798_comment'></div>奚畏奚不畏哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173798_comment'></div>丘明之言，使谀臣依以谄其君，邪臣资以固其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173798_comment'></div>臣请辨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173798_comment'></div>幽王之诗曰：「十月之交，朔日辛卯，日有食之，亦孔之丑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173798_comment'></div>周之十月，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1173798", 1173798, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>二分</span>矣，安在其不为灾者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173798_comment'></div>《夏书》曰：「乃季秋月朔，辰弗集于房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173798_comment'></div>瞽奏鼓，啬夫驰，庶人走」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173798_comment'></div>夏之季秋非正阳也，安在其不鼓者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173798_comment'></div>由此观之，日食之必可畏，必当救也，无所疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173798_comment'></div>夫谄谀奸邪之臣，出则朋党比周以遂其私，入则诐伪欺罔以济其欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173798_comment'></div>固日夜无须臾之间，惟恐君之觉己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173798_comment'></div>日有食之，是将喜焉，庸肯斥言灾异以儆于上哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173798_comment'></div>是以或至于陵夷，而犹不悟，鲁季孙、汉张禹是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173798_comment'></div>昔者季孙意如之专鲁，知日食之为伤其君而不忧也，卒逐昭公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173798_comment'></div>张禹之仕汉，知日食之为害国而不告也，卒成王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173798_comment'></div>呜呼，变所从来微矣，为人上者可不察哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173798_comment'></div>可不察哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1173798_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　是年作《读梅圣俞我今五十二诗感之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷八。）</span><div id='poem_497981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_497981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/497981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读圣俞我今五十二诗感之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_497981")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_497981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_497981'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_497981'>子真神仙吏，不识伤别离。<div id='poem_sentence_0_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_497981'>忽逢旧交叹，始悟人间悲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_497981'>岁月流水逝，富贵浮云驰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497981'>徘徊抚往事，感激吐新诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497981'>流水难以追，浮云难以推。<div id='poem_sentence_4_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_497981'>百年半如此，万事从可知。<div id='poem_sentence_5_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_497981'>且欲拂衣行，聊及鲈鱼期。<div id='poem_sentence_6_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_497981'>君若变名姓，相逢复何时。<div id='poem_sentence_7_497981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_497981'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_497981_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年1月</a>　正月，张贵妃薨，追号温成皇后，有献议求为立忌日，礼官请封不许，刘敞上《论温成立忌疏》谏之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论温成立忌疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173606")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173606'>臣伏闻敕旨，为温成皇后立忌，礼官请对不许，臣窃惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173606_comment'></div>凡朝廷常务，百司小事，犹当上稽旧典，下采众论，何况宗庙大礼，至尊至重，岂可以一时之宠，独决圣心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173606_comment'></div>义有僭失，贻笑万世，亏损盛明，悔不可追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173606_comment'></div>今议者乃云，有邪臣密启，眩惑圣聪，导陛下以非礼，劝陛下以拒谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173606_comment'></div>若此无实，倘非美事，设有其实，罪亦大矣，当伏两观之诛，以谢天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173606_comment'></div>且自太祖以来，后庙四室，皆陛下之妣也，犹不立忌，奈何以温成私昵之爱，变古越礼，则贵妾于妣，尊嬖于嫡，上无以事宗庙，下无以教后嗣，恐祖宗神灵不乐于此，非陛下奉先思孝之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173606_comment'></div>昔成汤改过不吝，故称圣王，格于皇天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173606_comment'></div>愿陛下毋笃于嬖近之宠，毋安于邪佞之说，毋变先帝之旧典，毋枉宗庙之正礼，回易意虑，却情去私，询于司存，追寝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1173606", 1173606, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>过命</span>，使万万亿年无复讥议，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173606_comment'></div>臣以无能，忝备儒馆，礼乐之失，臣得预言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1173606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年8月</a>　八月，同修起居注。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年9月</a>　九月召试，超拜右正言、知制诰，赐紫金鱼袋，权同判吏部流内铨，作《谢知制诰启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十五。）</span><div id='poem_1173729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173729?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知制诰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173729")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173729_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173729'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173729'>右，某启：蒙恩授前件职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173729_comment'></div>望卑而宠厚，能薄而选优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173729_comment'></div>内视缺如，自量幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173729_comment'></div>窃以三代之盛，溢于《诗》《书》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173729_comment'></div>两汉之隆，布在史册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173729_comment'></div>虽上德独茂，时文日新，亦有代言之臣，谋谟于内，秉笔之士，发挥于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173729_comment'></div>是以坟典粲然，若日星之华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173729_comment'></div>制度焕乎，有金玉之丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173729_comment'></div>兹体甚大，惟贤之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173729_comment'></div>而况皇图寖昌，妙虑臻极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173729_comment'></div>鼓天下者，悉独运于神化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173729_comment'></div>居廷中者，举绝望于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173729_comment'></div>将使少窥渊源，进赞名命，声教所被，八荒其同，训辞之传，万世无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173729_comment'></div>则宜得当代之杰，绝人之材，练达古今，发明贯变，矕秀龙虎，垂光虹蜺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173729_comment'></div>庶几相如视草之工，子产润色之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173729_comment'></div>若时述职，可以无惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173729_comment'></div>如某者，禀生颛蒙，执艺迂浅，径从诸儒之末，窃售一日之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173729_comment'></div>譬犹射非前期，难以称善中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173729_comment'></div>铸者跃冶，或以为不祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173729_comment'></div>然且玷甲乙之科，借交游之宠，通籍省户，飞缨蓬山，出入舆卫之间，编摩简牍之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173729_comment'></div>虽复自强，已非其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173729_comment'></div>岂可参法从之严，直右垣之秘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173729_comment'></div>此盖某官，乐兴善类，出于至诚，欲斲雕轮囷，以成大辂之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173729_comment'></div>驱策偃蹇，而效秋驾之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173729_comment'></div>故俾懦姿，遂肩荣选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173729_comment'></div>夫力不能进，则虽任鄙有绝膑之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173729_comment'></div>精非所堪，则虽颜生有皓发之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173729_comment'></div>然而僶俛奏技，徘徊就官，盖上答天施之隆，次酬己知之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173729_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1173729_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年10月</a>　十月，上《奔丧议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奔丧议</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173626")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173626'>臣窃见旧制，官自三司副使以上及班行使臣，遭父母丧者，例皆有百日公除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173626_comment'></div>孝子虽有思慕之心，犹逼于王命，不得遂行，此诚伤教害理，无取于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173626_comment'></div>臣伏以三年之丧，通于天下，以义制恩，古人有之，自谓身在军旅，躬被金革者，不敢以私事辞王事尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173626_comment'></div>本非承平之时，游谈侍从之臣所当行也，又非班行冗下之职所当预也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173626_comment'></div>习俗既久，寖以成风，其贤者则以不即人心为悲，其不肖者遂以当丧墨缞为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173626_comment'></div>以之锡类，是为伤恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173626_comment'></div>以之教民，是为忘孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173626_comment'></div>今天下往往有闻哀不举，废哀图仕，源自此始，不可不虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173626_comment'></div>传曰：「君子不夺人之亲，人亦不可夺亲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173626_comment'></div>窃谓惟在军中者，可权从变礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173626_comment'></div>其旧制三司副使以上及班行使臣百日公除，不合礼意，宜听行三年之服，以崇孝悌之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173626_comment'></div>臣又闻，古者大夫去国，三年然后收其田里，明有恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173626_comment'></div>今丁忧臣僚，即日绝其俸禄，亦为太薄，岂有行礼之人，反不及被放之臣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173626_comment'></div>臣往见丁忧者，家贫无食，乞丐糊口，其皇皇伤孝子之心，非所以化民成俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173626_comment'></div>臣以谓文官两制、武官自诸司使以上，与给全俸，其馀京官、班行使臣，与给半俸，以明朝廷笃于礼而厚于教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173626_comment'></div>乞下近臣商量可否。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1173626_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　十月，上《乞听百官服亲丧三年奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）失载。）</span><div id='poem_1173627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞听百官服亲丧三年奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173627")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173627_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173627'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173627'>陛下幸加恩令诸近臣得为亲服三年，又不夺其俸，至仁至惠，不可尚矣，然常参京朝官、班行使臣犹不用此令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173627_comment'></div>臣以为名位不同，尊亲一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173627_comment'></div>苟取周急，不宜分别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173627_comment'></div>《书》云：「无偏无党，王道荡荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173627_comment'></div>无党无偏，王道平平」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173627_comment'></div>惟陛下留意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1173627_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月</a>　十一月壬午，入内押班石全斌为入内副都知，敞对还词头，并上《论石全斌不当除入内副都知状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论石全斌不当除入内副都知状</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173621")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173621'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173621'>臣窃见入内押班石全斌，为入内副都知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173621_comment'></div>臣谨按，全斌昨已有制旨，除宫苑使、利州观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173621_comment'></div>未能三日，复换此命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173621_comment'></div>朝令夕改，古人所非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173621_comment'></div>若因全斌陈请，探其不满之意，曲徇所求，以悦其心，便是朝廷恩典未有定制，惟系宦官临时徼乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173621_comment'></div>宣布天下，必以为惑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173621_comment'></div>传示后世，必以为笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173621_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173621_comment'></div>陛下赏罚，当信天下，当教后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173621_comment'></div>不知全斌功勤凡有几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173621_comment'></div>昨者岭外之行，已曾受赏，今后温成葬毕，赏又不薄，不知厌足，愈求迁进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173621_comment'></div>朝廷亦当爱惜事体，无宜轻改成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173621_comment'></div>全斌闺闼之臣，尚如此姑息，万一复有权势重于全斌者，如何待之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173621_comment'></div>臣虽鄙贱，实惜此体，不敢辄撰告词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1173621_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　上《论吴充不当以谴责礼生被逐疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173589?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论吴充不当以谴责礼生被逐疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173589")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173589_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173589'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173589'>臣伏闻同知太常礼院吴充、鞠真卿并除知军差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173589_comment'></div>馆阁补郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173589_comment'></div>盖是常事，资序之间，亦无重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173589_comment'></div>今者，在外论议，皆云鞠真卿曾因自陈，先有指挥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173589_comment'></div>而吴充只缘公事，谴责礼生，以此迕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173589_comment'></div>不审虚实，但此声既布，此体可惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173589_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173589_comment'></div>吴充官则博士，职则礼院，朝廷欲有兴为，询求宜适，而胥吏辄敢擅发印状，曾不禀问，此则岂惟轻侮吴充而已，实亦上忽诏旨，在于事体，不得不怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173589_comment'></div>而太常寺长官初不纠按，开封府受牒，又曲为容庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173589_comment'></div>观此首尾，乃是礼生可诛，太常寺可责，开封府可劾，而吴充可赏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173589_comment'></div>今既未然，礼生一以赎论，礼官随而斥罢，自然众情不能无惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173589_comment'></div>朝廷久安，吏习因循，百司庶府，处处茍且，稍激厉振职，尚未有知如何，更行此事，恐浅近之徒，因以为戒，且见吴充以振举职事被谪，以谴劾胥吏被逐，不如茍且，岂不伤事、岂不害政哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173589_comment'></div>先王所以下酌民言，释疑止谤，盖为此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173589_comment'></div>伏望神慈，追正前命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173589_comment'></div>臣初拜官谢恩，面蒙开许，有不便事，得以奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173589_comment'></div>奉承以还，不敢失坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173589_comment'></div>窃谓外间此议，实称不便。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1173589'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1173589_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　两上《论大臣不当排言者疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173590' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173590' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173590?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论大臣不当排言者疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173590")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173590_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173590'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173590'>臣昨闻吴充黜官，冯京落职，将谓其人所行实有过当，所言实有不可，是以触忤圣意，不蒙矜恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173590_comment'></div>及于延和殿奏事，面奉宣谕，充乃是振职，京意亦无他，中书恶其太直，不与含容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173590_comment'></div>臣窃惊骇，不觉愤咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173590_comment'></div>前古以来，惟有人主不能容受直言，或致窜谪臣下，今陛下慈仁好谏，宽大如此，不知中书何故不思将顺圣意之美，要须排逐言者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173590_comment'></div>今四方之人不知本末，反谓陛下不能听谏，口谤腹诽，所损不小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173590_comment'></div>且如此事，陛下心所必恕，中书却欲必行，是蔽君之明，止君之善，侵君之权，增君之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173590_comment'></div>苟要作威，惊动朝望，今后虽有不公不直，人不敢言，得以利己，得以罔上，陛下不可不深察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173590_comment'></div>臣按六经、旧史，大臣蔽君之明，止君之善，侵君之权，增君之过者，皆为不忠，陷于刑诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173590_comment'></div>况今时人情，远不如古，若闻陛下欲为而牵于大臣，大臣欲作威而不惮陛下，则必相率背公向私，奔竞权门矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173590_comment'></div>此风一动，此势一失，是为君与臣同国，圣人之至戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173590_comment'></div>鲁僖公时，频致天旱，《春秋》谓由公子遂专权之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173590_comment'></div>而《洪范》五行：僭则常旸，蒙则常风，下侵上则山崩地震，日月薄蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173590_comment'></div>如今者此事，逆于伦理，必恐感动阴阳，或能遂致灾旱风雾、山崩地震，日月之眚，望陛下留神，深察此言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173590_comment'></div>臣以浅近，荷陛下厚恩，不敢不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173590_comment'></div>窃恨此一事，近世未有，臣虽口陈，未能详尽，谨手书具奏以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1173590_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　作《晏公挽词三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十二。）</span><div id='poem_498777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晏公挽词三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498777")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498777'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498777'>望苑牧英隽，岩廊奉德音。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498777'>功如四支重，化以二南深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498777'>安仰嗟维石，能传赖碎金。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498777'>浮云送哀挽，惨澹更为霖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498777'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498777_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_498778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498778?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498778'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498778'>简易能容士，精诚乐与贤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498778'>如何五湖上，非复赤松年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498778'>几几空遗舄，悠悠不问天。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498778'>独应春辍相，令望故依然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498778'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498778_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_498779' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498779' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498779?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498779_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498779'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498779'>衮韨三司旧，笳箫一品荣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498779'>独伤去国意，仍以抚封行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498779'>落日白驹影，空林黄鸟声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498779'>公归那不复，悽怆国人情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498779'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498779_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript:
