ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年4月</a>　四月，上《论孔宗愿袭文宣公》疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论孔宗愿袭文宣公疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173603")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173603'>臣等据祠部员外郎、直集贤院祖无择奏：「伏见至圣文宣王四十七代孙孔宗愿袭封文宣公，乃是其人未死，已赐谥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173603_comment'></div>臣窃观前史，孔子之后袭封者众，在汉魏则曰褒成、褒圣、宗圣，在晋、宋亦曰奉圣，后魏曰崇圣，北齐曰恭圣，后周及隋封以邹国，唐初曰褒圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173603_comment'></div>或为君，或为侯，为公，为大夫，使奉祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173603_comment'></div>唯汉平帝追谥孔子为褒成宣尼公，遂以均为褒成君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173603_comment'></div>至唐开元二十七年追谥为文宣王，又以其后为文宣公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173603_comment'></div>是皆以祖之美谥而加后嗣，生而谥之，不经甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173603_comment'></div>欲乞明诏有司，详求古训，或封以小国，或取尊儒褒圣之义，别定美号，加于封爵，著于令式，使千古之下无以加于我朝之盛典也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173603_comment'></div>右，奉圣旨，送两制详议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173603_comment'></div>臣等谨按，汉元帝初元元年，以师孔霸为关内侯，食邑八百户，号褒成君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173603_comment'></div>而霸上书，求奉孔子祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173603_comment'></div>元帝下诏曰：「其令师褒成君、关内侯霸以所食八百户祀孔子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173603_comment'></div>及霸卒，子福嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173603_comment'></div>福卒，子房嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173603_comment'></div>房卒，子莽嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173603_comment'></div>皆称褒成君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173603_comment'></div>平帝元光二年，始更以二千户封莽为褒成侯，而追谥孔子曰褒成宣尼公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173603_comment'></div>以此观之，则褒成者，国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173603_comment'></div>宣尼者，谥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173603_comment'></div>公侯者，爵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173603_comment'></div>褒成宣尼公者，犹曰河间献王云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173603_comment'></div>盖推宣尼以为褒成祖，非用褒成以为宣尼谥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173603_comment'></div>唐世不深察此义，以褒成为夫子之谥，因疑霸等封褒成者，皆袭其祖之旧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173603_comment'></div>故遂封夫子文宣王，而爵其后文宣公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173603_comment'></div>考校本末，甚失事理，因循承袭，至今不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173603_comment'></div>先帝既封泰山，亲祀阙里，又加文宣以至圣之号，则人伦之极致，盛德之显名，尽在此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173603_comment'></div>尤非其子孙臣庶所宜袭处而称之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173603_comment'></div>臣等以为无择议是，可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173603_comment'></div>其文宣王四十代孙孔宗愿，伏乞改赐爵名，若「褒成」、「奉圣」之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173603_comment'></div>上足以尊显先圣，有不阶之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173603_comment'></div>下不失优礼孔氏，使得守继世之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173603_comment'></div>改唐之失，法汉之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173603_comment'></div>传曰：「必也正名乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173603_comment'></div>又曰「正稽古立事，可以永年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173603_comment'></div>此类之谓也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1173603_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年4月</a>　四月，上《论水旱之本》疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论水旱之本疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173596")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173596'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173596'>臣伏见城中近日流民甚多，皆扶老携幼，无复生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173596_comment'></div>问其所从来，或云久旱，耕种失业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173596_comment'></div>或云河溢，田庐荡尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173596_comment'></div>窃闻圣慈悯其如此，多方救济，此诚陛下为民父母之意，足以感动群心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173596_comment'></div>臣犹谓但可宽目前之急而已，非救本之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173596_comment'></div>譬如良药疗病，必先审其病源，病源不除，强食无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173596_comment'></div>今百姓之病已可见矣，父子兄弟不能相保，鳏寡孤独不能自存，强者流转，弱者死亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173596_comment'></div>所以致此者，其源在水旱也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173596_comment'></div>所以致水旱者，其本在阴阳不和也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173596_comment'></div>所以致阴阳不和者，其端在人事不修也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173596_comment'></div>然则三公之职，主和阴阳，而议臣之任，主明天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173596_comment'></div>陛下何不责三公以其职，使之陈阴阳不和之理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173596_comment'></div>询议臣以其学，使之述天人相与之际，参之圣心，以观今日政事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173596_comment'></div>若陛下所委任皆已得人，所施皆已应天，则水旱者，盖无妄之灾，不足畏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173596_comment'></div>若天人之际少有不合，岂得晏然坐视其病，心知其源，不思救之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173596_comment'></div>臣言似迂，其理实切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173596_comment'></div>今群臣为陛下谋者，不过煮粥粜米，名为救济，其实亦欲欺聪明，自解免而已，非谋国之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173596_comment'></div>又今天气当暑反寒，率多常风，雨泽愆候，秋成不可必，愿陛下速思所以救其本者，召致和气，无令圣心重增焦劳，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1173596_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月</a>　六月，上《论邪正》疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173580?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论邪正疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173580")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173580'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173580'>臣伏以驭臣之道，在分别邪正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173580_comment'></div>正臣当亲而近之，邪臣当疏而远之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173580_comment'></div>至于天下之人，亦皆以此窥朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173580_comment'></div>若正臣聚于朝，则奸雄屏息，治平可望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173580_comment'></div>若邪臣聚于朝，则侥倖竞进，倾败可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173580_comment'></div>二者不可不深察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173580_comment'></div>臣伏观朝廷太平积久，贤能众多，然其间邪正，亦杂有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173580_comment'></div>或爱君忧国，非公正不发愤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173580_comment'></div>或朋党比周，背公树私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173580_comment'></div>亦有循默自守，不能为善，又不敢为恶者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173580_comment'></div>陛下临御三十馀年矣，以上圣之姿，鉴群下所为，固无遁形，固无隐情，然有可戒慎者，在此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173580_comment'></div>凡正臣常难进而易退，邪臣常易进而难退，何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173580_comment'></div>正臣者，惟义所在，言则逆君之耳，是所以难进也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173580_comment'></div>言或不用，不欲自显，因事而去，是所以易退也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173580_comment'></div>邪臣者，惟利所在，言则逢君之欲，是所以易进也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173580_comment'></div>行虽恶，不顾礼义，名虽丑，不知愧耻，患失之耳，是所以难退也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173580_comment'></div>此两臣者，愿陛下参伍观之，毋使当亲者疏，当疏者亲，则朝廷尊荣，而社稷安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173580_comment'></div>近者翰林侍读学士吕溱、枢密直学士蔡襄继出典郡，今又闻御史中丞孙抃、翰林学士欧阳修、知制诰贾黯、韩绛，并乞补外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173580_comment'></div>此其人等，皆有直质，无邪心，议论不阿执政，有益当世者也，诚不宜许之，使四方有以窥朝廷，而奸佞侥倖之雄因而竞起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173580_comment'></div>此则分别邪正之一端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173580_comment'></div>臣以孤拙，忝官侍从，日夜思维，无以少裨聪明，恐陛下忽于正臣之易退，而忘左右前后直道之不容也，不胜其愚，谨献所闻，惟赐采择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1173580_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年7月</a>　七月，上《迁官降官不宜单用敕》（《论除降不用诰》）疏。）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迁官降官不宜单用敕牒奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173629")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173629_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173629'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173629'>伏见故事，迁官降官，皆特有诰命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173629_comment'></div>前年因言事黜御史吴中复，其时蔡襄当草制，封还词头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173629_comment'></div>执政耻为所沮，遂单用敕牒降官，甚非故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173629_comment'></div>然有司不敢发明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173629_comment'></div>近日龙图阁直学士任颛落职，复但降敕劄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173629_comment'></div>因循习熟，遂成近例，事出一时，非政体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173629_comment'></div>欲乞今后除改命令，须遵用故事，合用诰词者不宜单降敕劄，务存旧法，有所沮劝，</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1173629_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年7月</a>　七月，上《论外官亲戚相代劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173625' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173625?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论外官亲戚相代劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173625")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173625'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173625'>臣伏见审官、三班、流内铨注拟外官，其间或兄弟伯叔子侄自相为代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173625_comment'></div>若前人政善，后人继之，善固无可言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173625_comment'></div>设前人政恶，后人因循之，则害政而负于义，如发举之，则伤恩而戾于教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173625_comment'></div>二者俱不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173625_comment'></div>即令前人有吏民之怨，因以去位，而后人怀亲戚之耻，乘之报忿，则一郡一邑，为害必多，非所以安细民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173625_comment'></div>臣谓审官、三班、流内铨所注拟外官，其在五服之内，于法许相容隐者，皆不得相为代，有敢妄冒居之者，以私罪论，于理为便。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1173625_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　是年，看详王讼《春秋通义》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='dc77c440f96b46d89ea2823a24fa0a73_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dc77c440f96b46d89ea2823a24fa0a73");'><span id='dc77c440f96b46d89ea2823a24fa0a73_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，38岁</div><div id='dc77c440f96b46d89ea2823a24fa0a73' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年闰3月</a>　闰三月，王尧臣参知政事，敞以亲嫌，求知扬州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　将赴扬州时，请出狄青，至后，仍议此事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6c735b00de2a449597ff2e885ba070ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6c735b00de2a449597ff2e885ba070ef");'><span id='6c735b00de2a449597ff2e885ba070ef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1060')">1058-1060年</a>，40-42岁</div><div id='6c735b00de2a449597ff2e885ba070ef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年11月</a>　十一月，召还朝，纠察在京刑狱，充宗正司修玉牒官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年12月</a>　十二月，受诏与胡宿详定官制，两上《辞不受详定官制劄子》，不允。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　十二月，受诏与胡宿详定官制，上《受敕后奏乞先条数事与中书门下更加商量劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　十二月，受诏与胡宿详定官制，上《条上详定官制事件劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>条上详定官制事件劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173614")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173614'>臣等昨奉敕，为翰林学士韩绛上言，国家奄有四海，承平百年，官制未修，方苦其陋，欲望讨论唐百官制及本朝官制品秩事件，量加裁定，正其名体等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173614_comment'></div>奉旨差臣等同共详定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173614_comment'></div>臣等累曾恳辞，不蒙允许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173614_comment'></div>寻具劄子陈乞，且未置局，容臣等取前代官制，将今日官品职位，商度可改正者，可裁损者，可申明者，各条三两事，先送中书门下，更加商量，若果可施行，即制局辟官，次第删奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173614_comment'></div>圣旨：依奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173614_comment'></div>臣等今详定到事件如左：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1173614'>一、汉置丞相，其后改置三公，官皆公府，辟召掾属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173614_comment'></div>唐制，以尚书、门下，中书三省长官为宰相，尚书令、仆射、侍中、中书令是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173614_comment'></div>官品未至者，同中书门下三品，今平章事即其比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173614_comment'></div>参知政事，唐初亦是正相，崔、温等尝为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173614_comment'></div>国朝之制，下宰相一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173614_comment'></div>若用唐制，正其名体，则四辅之任当悉用平章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173614_comment'></div>依汉制，即须立丞相府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1173614'>一、唐制，御史大夫一人，中丞三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173614_comment'></div>国朝之制，大夫不置，以中丞为台长，他官或以给事中、谏议大夫权之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173614_comment'></div>若欲改正官制，置丞相府，则大夫当复，轻重乃等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1173614'>一、唐制无公卿为枢密事，五代用兵，始与中书对掌机密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173614_comment'></div>欲改正官制，当以院事还中书及尚书兵部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1173614'>一、尚书省二十四司既为虚名，所以官冗员众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173614_comment'></div>即欲改正官制，当罢三司，复二十四司及九卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173614_comment'></div>官使有定员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173614_comment'></div>其郎官不在本省治职事者，并以前资及散官处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173614_comment'></div>其涖外任者，或依唐制，置上中下等州刺史及别驾之类，随官品任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173614_comment'></div>或欲轻其权，则曰知某州刺史之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1173614'>一、文武散官及检校、兼官、勋、爵、实封等，在开元已前，颇有实事，于今为散官，犹叙服色，粗系轻重，其馀悉皆虚名，无益治体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173614_comment'></div>即欲改正官制，当例行省罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173614_comment'></div>若以假虚名而任实职，兼存亦可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1173614'>已上所谓改正者也，略举一隅，若于今可行，即推此类具正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1173614'>一、大理寺决天下之狱，刑部覆之，于事已足，又加审刑院，则为骈衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173614_comment'></div>即欲裁损官制，当以院事官属还刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1173614'>一、吏部尚书、侍郎，分领铨事，则当差以轻重，分别流品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173614_comment'></div>今审官院掌京朝官磨勘差遣，而流内铨惟典州县幕职官，体制不伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173614_comment'></div>即欲裁损官制，当以审官院职事归尚书铨，州县幕职官归侍郎铨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1173614'>一、群牧司、提举司、观察司之类，皆古无此职，即欲裁损官制，悉当省罢，还属尚书九卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173614_comment'></div>已上所谓裁损者也，略举一隅，若于今可行，即推此类具正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1173614'>一、左右史并当随宰相入立仗下，以记言动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173614_comment'></div>今史官之任，不及闻前殿正事，故德音善政，多失纪录，欲申明复此旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1173614'>一、中书出制敕，唐制并经门下审覆，然后尚书出告身，经历三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173614_comment'></div>比来惟于中书发敕，虚置三省官名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173614_comment'></div>今欲申明复此制，国朝令文具载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1173614'>一、国朝近制，观文殿大学士惟待旧相，自资政殿大学士，至天章阁待制已上，其间多有无员数，数除受侵广者，由边幅不立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1173614_comment'></div>诸旧有员者，宜依旧数，未有者，宜差定其员，著为久制，以革一员之滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1173614'>一、唐制，舍人六人，分判尚书六曹事，所以佐丞相，谨政令，欲乞申明此制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1173614'>一、旧制，九卿之职，不隶尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1173614_comment'></div>今卿监职事三司关领者，宜取还寺，亦省侵官之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1173614'>一、唐制，左右丞相判尚书省事，中书判门下省事，中书舍人判中书省事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1173614_comment'></div>国朝门下省权用近臣判之，中书省即舍人年深者判，与唐制略同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1173614_comment'></div>准昨来言者称，近臣判省太重，考按唐制，似不如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1173614_comment'></div>惟常衮自以同中书门下事，即当兼判中书省，是时崔祐甫以舍人判省，谓衮侵官，士论由此不平衮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1173614'>一、三班自供奉官至殿侍差使之类，唐制武选皆无此名目，宜徙置于外，以区别华冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1173614'>一、朝廷若从改正之说，即俟改正之后，设官分职如周、唐，乃可约六典著书，垂之后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1173614_comment'></div>若未能如此，而欲著书，惟可将会要及诸司编敕并格令，删繁取要，因今日官名粗书职分而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1173614_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1173614'>已上所谓申明者也，略举一隅，若于今可行，即推此类具正之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1173614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年12月</a>　12月，再游会灵观，作《辛卯十二月同持国游会灵观各曾赋诗后一年会灵烧高下俱尽天子为先朝所为不忍废复治集禧略放渭阳帝祠制度五岳同宇毋乏事而已不能如向之钜丽也戊戌十二月以事过谒祠下作七言寄持国》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十九。）</span><div id='poem_499263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛卯十二月同持国游会灵观各曾赋诗后一年会灵烧高下俱尽天子为先朝所为不忍废复治集禧略放渭阳帝祠制度五岳同宇毋乏事而已不能如向之钜丽也戊戌十二月以事过谒祠下作七言寄持国</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_499263")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_499263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_499263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_499263'>白玉五城十二楼，还曾同作采真游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_499263'>重来无复壶中景，惟见苍林锁碧流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_499263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_499263'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_499263_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年闰12月</a>　闰十二月己卯，诏明年正旦日食，其自丁亥避正殿，减常膳，燕契丹使无作乐，敞上《论元日合朔避寝太早劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论元日合朔避寝太早劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（嘉祐三年闰十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年闰12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173588")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173588'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173588'>臣窃闻朝议，以元旦合朔，欲自二十一日避正殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173588_comment'></div>臣以谓天明虽有可畏之道，然亦当稽古率礼，然后为允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173588_comment'></div>按三代之典，日食无豫避之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173588_comment'></div>《左氏传》称避移时，《曾子问》诸侯入门，不得行礼者，日食居其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173588_comment'></div>此皆睹有变而戒，非蚤备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173588_comment'></div>先王制礼，过之者犹不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173588_comment'></div>其制法，先时者与不及时者，均贵得中而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173588_comment'></div>汉唐素服寝兵，却朝会不视事，及求直言，大率皆在合朔之辰，未有先时旬日者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173588_comment'></div>兆忧太过，《春秋》所讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173588_comment'></div>今敌使来朝，远方观礼，举措失中，或轻为所觇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173588_comment'></div>伏乞详求旧典，折衷于礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173588_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1173588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　甲申，受诏视真宗庙室。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　是年，作《答令狐司封使君舟中见寄》诗，末注[某戊子春与使君会汝南，到今适十年]<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十四。毕仲游《西台集》卷十二有《司封员外郎令狐公墓志铭》，据此文可知令狐司封即令狐挺。）</span><div id='poem_498892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答令狐司封使君舟中见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498892")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498892'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498892'>汝颍相从弥十年，江楼今日迟归船。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498892'>自惊物役还如昔，但觉诗情更爽然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498892'>寥落莺花千骑里，苍茫烟雨万山前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498892'>未知后会仍何地，彊醉春风酒似泉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498892'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498892'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_498892_0'>⑴ 自注：某戊子春与使君会汝南，到今适十年。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498892_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年1月</a>　正月丙申朔，日食，遣官祭社，刘敞上《论日食用牲于社非礼疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论日食用牲于社非礼疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173608")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173608'>臣前论先期避殿不中古典，未蒙省察；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173608_comment'></div>今又闻遣官祭社，稽之于经，亦未见此礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173608_comment'></div>盖社者，上公之神，群阴之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173608_comment'></div>故日食则伐鼓于社，所以责上公，退群阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173608_comment'></div>今反祠而请之，是屈天子之礼，从诸侯之制，抑阳扶阴，降尊贬重，非承天戒、尊朝廷之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173608_comment'></div>且礼者先王训民事君，不可不谨，前事之失，习俗未久，苟为因循，则宪章废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173608_comment'></div>惟陛下稽古正名，审所施为，毋以礼假人也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1173608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年1月</a>　同权知贡举，得宋仁宗赐墨字[稽古]之赞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年1月</a>　刘敞作《诏赐御书稽古两字作口号示子弟》，末注：“于时予知贡举，又纠察刑狱。”<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十九。）</span><div id='poem_499252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诏赐御书稽古两字作口号示子弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_499252")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_499252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_499252'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_499252'>毛玠素屏非俗物，韩棱宝剑得龙渊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_499252'>谟明敢与皋陶比，稽古虚参尧舜篇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_499252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_499252'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_499252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_499252'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_499252_0'>⑴ 自注：于时予知贡举，又纪察刑狱。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_499252_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年2月</a>　二月，刘敞奏请减罢郓齐等州管界巡检及驻兵，诏从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年3月</a>　三月，韩绛奏请详定官制，刘敞与胡宿诣政事堂，言其不可。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年4月</a>　四月壬辰，宋仁宗以皇女生御崇政殿录系囚杂犯死罪以下递降一等，徒以下释之，刘敞上《论皇女生疏决赐予疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论皇女生疏决赐予疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173595")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173595'>臣伏见今月二十八日，疏决在京系囚，虽恩出一时，然在外群情，皆云圣意以皇女生，故赐庆泽，恐非王者之令典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173595_comment'></div>去年闰月，已曾减降，尚未半年，复行此恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173595_comment'></div>《传》称「民之多幸，则于国不幸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173595_comment'></div>一岁再赦，好人喑哑，前世明君贤臣论此详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173595_comment'></div>虽成事不说，臣愿朝廷戒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173595_comment'></div>又闻多作金银、犀象、玉石、琥珀、玳瑁、檀香等钱，及铸金银为花果，赐予臣下，自宰相、台谏皆受此赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173595_comment'></div>臣谓陛下无益之赐，无名之赏，殆无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173595_comment'></div>若夸示奢丽，臣以辅主为职，奈何空受此赐，曾无一言焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173595_comment'></div>遂事不谏，臣愿陛下戒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173595_comment'></div>伏惟皇上开祐圣德，故后宫有多子之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173595_comment'></div>陛下当明谨政令，深执恭俭，以答上天之贶，建无疆之基，不宜行姑息之恩，以损政体，出浮冗之费，以隳俭德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173595_comment'></div>臣虽鄙浅，窃独惜此，故敢触冒陈闻，惟赐裁幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1173595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年6月</a>　六月己巳，宰臣富弼等请加宋仁宗尊号“大仁至治”，刘敞上《乞固辞徽号疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞固辞徽号疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173592")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173592'>臣伏见宰臣率文武百官诣东上閤门拜表乞加上尊号，准批答不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173592_comment'></div>此诚见陛下恭逊持满、恶盈好谦之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173592_comment'></div>且陛下自宝元以来，不复加徽号，近二十馀年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173592_comment'></div>冲逊之德，上通于天，下信于民，此上天所以保祐圣躬，受福无疆，万民所以爱载圣政，日新一日者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173592_comment'></div>今实不须稍增数字，示人自满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173592_comment'></div>臣窃愿陛下固执雅意，群臣虽十上表，坚逊勿受，足以益见积年冲逊之实，必大得天人之祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173592_comment'></div>且陛下尊号既已云「体天法道钦文聪武圣神孝德」，尽善极美矣，复曰「大仁」，不足增光，而曰「至治」，则有若自矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173592_comment'></div>今百姓多困，仓廪不实，风俗未清，贤否混淆，狱讼繁多，盗贼群辈，水旱继有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173592_comment'></div>虽四夷初定，然本以重赂厚利羁縻而服之，非畏威慕义者也，未可谓「至治」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173592_comment'></div>然则逊而不居，于圣德弥高矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173592_comment'></div>今群臣皆以加上徽号为请，而臣独望陛下以固辞徽号为愿，其心则同欲尊君，同欲爱君，然望陛下裁之圣虑，参之美志，断而行之，则有高世之名，与道同符，岂数字可尽哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1173592_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年7月</a>　七月，上《论京师刑狱当委纠察司澄审状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1173631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论京师刑狱当委纠察司澄审状</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173631")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173631'>先帝仁圣钦恤，以京师刑狱最繁，故建纠察一司，澄审真伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173631_comment'></div>自尔以来，每有大辟，倍加精审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173631_comment'></div>此则先帝不敢兼于庶狱庶慎，惟有司之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173631_comment'></div>今乃曲忤圣旨，中书门下、枢密院所鞫公事，不复审察，未见所以尊朝廷，审刑罚，而适足启府县弛慢，狱吏侵侮，罪人衔冤不得告诉之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173631_comment'></div>又朝廷旧法，不许用例破条，今顾于刑狱极谨、人命至重之际，而废条用例，此臣所不喻也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1173631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　上《论纠察司劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谕纠察司劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173610")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173610'>臣伏以先帝哀矜庶狱，开释无辜，以京师浩穰，狱讼繁多，创设纠察一司，辨理微枉，澄审谬误，诚不欲使吏得弄法，民陷非罪，设令侵冤，有所告诉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173610_comment'></div>伏见诸大辟公事，或具狱既上，情涉可疑，或审问之际，因自翻变者，并皆移司推勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173610_comment'></div>左军则移右军，右军则移左军，府司亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173610_comment'></div>然此三处形势既均，利害略同，更相顾望，自为地道，宁伸吏曲，莫念民枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173610_comment'></div>以此治狱，恐非朝廷钦恤之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173610_comment'></div>臣谓诸大辟公事，其情理可疑及囚自变者，并委纠察司奏请，别差官置勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173610_comment'></div>其司狱等，仍须与元勘处不相干碍，方许抽差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173610_comment'></div>如此，则狱无衔冤之滥，吏无试法之倖，好生之德，洽于民心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173610_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1173610_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年8月</a>　八月，上《论郭后不当祔庙疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《历代名臣奏议》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1173632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论郭后不当祔庙疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173632")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173632'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173632'>伏闻礼官倡议，欲祔郭后于庙，臣窃惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173632_comment'></div>昔《春秋》之义：「夫人不薨于寝，不赴于同，不反哭于庙，则不言夫人，不称小君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173632_comment'></div>徒以礼不足，故名号阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173632_comment'></div>然则名与礼，非同物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173632_comment'></div>名号存而礼不足，因不敢正其称，况敢正其仪乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173632_comment'></div>郭后之废，虽云无大罪，然亦既废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173632_comment'></div>及其追复也，许其号而不许其礼，且二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173632_comment'></div>今一旦欲施以嫡后之仪，致之于庙，然则郭氏之殂也，为薨于寝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173632_comment'></div>赴于同乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173632_comment'></div>反哭于庙乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173632_comment'></div>群臣百姓亦尝以服母之义为之齐衰乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173632_comment'></div>恐其未安于《春秋》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173632_comment'></div>《春秋》，夫人于彼三者一不备，则不正其称，而郭后于三者无一焉，而欲正其礼，恐其未安于义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173632_comment'></div>《春秋》：「禘于太庙，用致夫人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173632_comment'></div>盖以为致者，不宜致也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173632_comment'></div>不宜致者，以其不薨于寝，不祔于姑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173632_comment'></div>且《传》曰：「不有废也，君何以兴」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173632_comment'></div>废兴之间，故必有正与不正之理存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173632_comment'></div>今欲扶所废以为正，亦将抑所兴以为不正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173632_comment'></div>古者不二嫡，则万世之后，宗庙之礼，岂臣子所当擅轻重哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173632_comment'></div>谨案景祐诏书，本不许郭氏祔庙，议已决矣，无为复纷纷以乱大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173632_comment'></div>议者或谓郭后追命也，诏书薄其过，既复其号，不得不异其礼，譬犹大臣坐非辜而贬者，茍明其非辜，则复用之，岂得不遂使为大臣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173632_comment'></div>夫物有殊类异势，未可以相准者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173632_comment'></div>臣之与妻，其义虽均，然逐臣可以复归，放妻不可复合，臣众而妻一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173632_comment'></div>故《春秋》公孙婴齐卒于狸脤，君曰：「吾固许之反为大夫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173632_comment'></div>此逐臣可以复归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173632_comment'></div>杞伯来逆叔姬之丧以归，夫无迎出妻之丧而为尔者，此放妻不可复合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173632_comment'></div>今追祔郭后，得无近于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173632_comment'></div>乞令诸儒博议，极其论难，以求折衷，于礼为允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1173632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1173632'><span class='label'>按：</span>《太常因革礼》卷一○○。又见《续资治通鉴长编》卷一九○，《宋会要辑稿》礼一○之六。第一册第五五○页《历代名臣奏议》卷一九，《续资治通鉴》卷五八，《江右文钞》卷一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1173632_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　张洞上疏驳刘敞《论郭后不当祔庙疏》意见，刘敞又上《再论郭后不当祔庙兼驳张洞疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《历代名臣奏议》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1173633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论郭后不当祔庙兼驳张洞疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173633")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173633'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173633'>近上言郭后追祔非正，乞更详议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173633_comment'></div>今月七日，学士院以张洞奏状示臣，准中书批状，令两制同议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173633_comment'></div>臣以所论与洞不合，更不连书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173633_comment'></div>然臣观洞之言，曼辞饰说，似茍欲蔽前之失，非忠信之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173633_comment'></div>前世之君，废斥妃后者，皆溺于私爱，或嬖妾上僭，或谗诉妄及，此群臣皆引大礼伏节死争，如陛下于郭后，固未尝有此，盖于时圣虑在宗庙社稷之际，不得不然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173633_comment'></div>昔光武起于布衣，绍复天位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173633_comment'></div>郭氏，其后也，正位十有六年，子彊为太子，子辅为中山王，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173633_comment'></div>然自见年长宠衰，数怀怨怼，光武由此废之为中山王太后，其后太子彊亦自贬引为东海王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173633_comment'></div>然当时文武大臣，元功俊德，布于朝廷，不以光武为情有厚薄，亦不以郭氏为过不当废者，意其识深远，知事不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173633_comment'></div>今陛下之虑，岂不然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173633_comment'></div>光武虽废郭氏，然顾待其家，初不衰减，亦明退人以义，不缘于私故也，此又诏书所以追复郭后之意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173633_comment'></div>用平生之爱，故尊以虚名，顾礼义之正，故绝其祔庙，是范晔所谓使后世不见隆薄进退之隙者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173633_comment'></div>至公至平，可谓折中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173633_comment'></div>今洞之意，以追复郭后，则出于天子，以停止庙谥，则出于大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173633_comment'></div>共一诏书也，而论之异同，未知洞何从见之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173633_comment'></div>若不幸而此言传于后，且归过君父，亏损圣德，此其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173633_comment'></div>且臣前奏最要切者，以谓废兴不两立，而人君无二嫡，备万世之后而礼分不明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173633_comment'></div>洞既不以此为辨，若不幸朝廷过听之，是虽自以能讦上起废为功，而犹且阴偪母后，妄渎正礼，此其二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173633_comment'></div>故臣以谓非臣子之义、忠信之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173633_comment'></div>伏乞并下臣章，令两制详议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173633_comment'></div>臣诚愚妄，窃耻圣朝无光武之臣，是以莫能推明上德，而反崇饰诽谤，营为非礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173633_comment'></div>不胜区区，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1173633_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年8月</a>　八月癸未，上《论龙昌期学术乖僻疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论龙昌期学术乖僻疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173601")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173601'>臣闻人主所谨，一嚬一笑，诚以众人所望视，天下所仿效者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173601_comment'></div>古者圣王之行赏也，服物之章，不可倖得，府库之财，不以滥予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173601_comment'></div>前日朝廷以龙昌期所著书下两制，臣等观其穿凿臆说，诡僻不经，甚至毁訾周公，疑误后学，难以示远，乞下益州，毁弃板本，未闻朝廷卓然有所施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173601_comment'></div>今忽加赐五品章服，及绢百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173601_comment'></div>臣未知谁主为奸邪，崇伪饰虚，附下罔上，以误陛下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173601_comment'></div>执政又曾不能谨重政体，顾畏公议，茍慰藉人情，卖弄国恩，其失岂特嚬笑之间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173601_comment'></div>按昌期之书，违古背道，所谓言伪而辨，学非而博，是王制之不听而诛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173601_comment'></div>陛下哀其衰老，未便服少正卯之刑则幸矣，又何赏之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173601_comment'></div>昔孔子作《孝经》，以非圣人者无法，乃比不孝之罪、要君之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173601_comment'></div>而朝廷顾多昌期之毁周公，臣所不晓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173601_comment'></div>且陛下使臣等议之，臣等不敢不尽忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173601_comment'></div>既而弃其言焉，岂以臣等为蔽贤而害能乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173601_comment'></div>夫蔽贤而害能，人臣之大罪也，愿陛下因正臣等之罪，而大表显昌期之书，使天下皆服诵而习尚之，则可以释谤于万世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173601_comment'></div>自非然者，置臣等之言而不用，纵昌期之妄而不诛，乃反褒以命服，厚以重币，是非贸乱，沮劝颠倒，使迷国之计行于侧，而非圣人之俗倡于下，臣窃为陛下不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173601_comment'></div>《书》曰：「天命有德，五服五章哉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173601_comment'></div>夫章服固天所有，而财力又民之所出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173601_comment'></div>陛下奈何曲徇大臣之意，而茍荣小人之身乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173601_comment'></div>将使远方寡见浅闻之民，奔走于辨伪之学，沈没于非圣人之论，迷而不反，非国家之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173601_comment'></div>伏乞追还诏书，断天下之疑议，毋使有识之士，窥朝廷之浅深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173601_comment'></div>臣不胜拳拳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1173601_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年8月</a>　与孙抃、胡宿等上《论孝惠四后袷祭合食四疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《续资治通鉴长编》卷一九〇。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年9月</a>　九月，撰《吕溱落职分司制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《宋大诏令集》卷二〇五。）</span><div id='poem_1173578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕溱落职分司制</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173578")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173578'>有司：吕溱前在真定，委信小吏，至假官曲酿酒，又使人诣旁郡贸易私利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173578_comment'></div>朕惟溱简直好节，立身有本末，其推诚不疑，使吏陷之法，不欲寘于理，以厉在位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173578_comment'></div>解溱近职，分务别都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173578_comment'></div>溱之浚明高爽，固必有以矫其前失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173578_comment'></div>朕亦不以一眚废，尔其勉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173578_comment'></div>可落翰林侍读学士，依前礼部郎中分司南京。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1173578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月</a>　十月，上《论景灵宫不当建郭后影殿疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论景灵宫不当建郭后影殿疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173602")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173602'>臣所领礼院得御药公文，称奉圣旨，送画到景灵宫广孝殿后，建郭皇后影殿图子一本详定者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173602_comment'></div>其图子已别具状缴奏讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173602_comment'></div>臣伏见近日京师木土之功，靡耗国用，其弊特深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173602_comment'></div>原其本因，只为差内臣监修，利于偷窃官物，及讫功之后，侥求恩赏，以故多起事端，务广兴作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173602_comment'></div>其甚则托以祖宗神御，张皇事势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173602_comment'></div>近年以来，如此兴造，略无虚岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173602_comment'></div>伏以景灵宫建自先朝，以尊奉圣祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173602_comment'></div>陛下又建真宗皇帝、章懿太后神御殿于其间，天下之人皆知陛下奉先广孝之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173602_comment'></div>然则此宫乃陛下奉亲之所，今乃欲以后宫已废未复之后，建殿与先帝太后并列，有渎神灵，莫此之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173602_comment'></div>臣窃谓事决不出于圣意，皆小人私与兴作，有所侥求尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173602_comment'></div>盖自前世，帝王于宗庙之外别为庙享，以追奉祖宗者则有之，未闻有自追奉其妃后者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173602_comment'></div>盖小人不识事体，但茍一时之利，不思损亏圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173602_comment'></div>伏乞特赐寝罢，以全典礼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1173602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月</a>　仁宗亲袷祭太庙，礼毕，刘敞加恩上骑都尉，进封开国子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月</a>　是月，为舅氏王冲撰《尚书屯田郎中提举兖州仙源县景灵宫王公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173930' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173930?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书屯田郎中提举兖州仙源县景灵宫王公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173930")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173930'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173930'>公讳冲，字景儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173930_comment'></div>其先自太原迁宋，居虞城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173930_comment'></div>祖化，赠太傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173930_comment'></div>考砺，赠太师、中书令，于今为显家，故弗论著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173930_comment'></div>公少则好学，论议依名节，慷慨自喜，不与众浮沉，士友多惮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173930_comment'></div>祥符中，举服勤词学，成进士名，得试校书郎，知兴国军永兴县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173930_comment'></div>父丧解官，服除，选于吏部，试判优等，为武安军掌书记，授武昌军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173930_comment'></div>崇阳民陈广与人斗，斗者以他疾死，而吏劾广杀人，议寘大辟，广亦不能自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173930_comment'></div>公擿其状以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173930_comment'></div>有诏下旁郡覆广狱，广卒无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173930_comment'></div>转运使奇其意，欲为之请赏，公辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173930_comment'></div>天圣初，改著作佐郎，知寿州霍丘县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173930_comment'></div>吏积不治，盗贼放横，公使其百姓邻伍相收司，而以耳目一切纠发老奸宿逋，岁中尽服，禽无脱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173930_comment'></div>徙蜀州晋源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173930_comment'></div>改秘书丞，知陈留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173930_comment'></div>当是时，章献太后垂帘听朝，而中人用事者罗崇勋之徒，交通县豪，借之意气，以渔夺细民，吏不敢问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173930_comment'></div>公独以法绳之，请谒无所听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173930_comment'></div>大姓田滋等由此惧，造飞语以奸利事污公，太后果怒，下公吏，使中人杂治之，讯掠甚急，欲公自诬服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173930_comment'></div>公义不屈，宁必死，不肯少自下，狱遂不具，然犹坐除名，徙雷州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173930_comment'></div>景祐初，上始亲政，尽斥逐罗崇勋等，诸附丽之者亦贬废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173930_comment'></div>言事者多以公不辜闻，天子亦自识其名，复起为卫尉寺丞，又诏尽雪向罪，后勿用以为负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173930_comment'></div>改著作佐郎，知越州会稽县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173930_comment'></div>都巡检使张怀信所部兵乱，百姓恟惧，欲逃入山谷间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173930_comment'></div>公策其不足虞，固请彻城门兵，以坚众心，郡中由是安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173930_comment'></div>康定初，复为秘书丞，通判乾州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173930_comment'></div>自元昊畔，边将数战不利，而民力以屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173930_comment'></div>公上《备边》、《御戎》等策，及言复郑国渠以实关中，事遂施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173930_comment'></div>通判华州，月馀，擢知乾州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173930_comment'></div>迁太常博士，知洋州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173930_comment'></div>真符县言，民家失火，举族焚死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173930_comment'></div>公视其状，曰：「必仇者为之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173930_comment'></div>教吏推迹其人，与三日期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173930_comment'></div>贼果得，一郡大惊，以为神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173930_comment'></div>郡故无学，公为立黉舍，收其才子弟，得二三十人，亲教养之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173930_comment'></div>吏观听悦喜，由此彬彬然兴于学，与西州等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173930_comment'></div>迁屯田员外郎、知泰州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173930_comment'></div>明年，改都官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173930_comment'></div>岁饥，发常平仓以食饥者，凡所活数万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173930_comment'></div>使者上其治为淮南第一，赐绯衣、鱼符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173930_comment'></div>改职方，领南京留司御史台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1173930_comment'></div>就迁屯田郎中，提举兖州仙源县景灵宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1173930_comment'></div>受诏未行，嘉祐元年十一月甲子以疾终，年六十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1173930_comment'></div>后三年十月甲子，葬某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1173930_comment'></div>初，公起黄绶，至二千石，更四县五州，所居见纪，未尝官京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1173930_comment'></div>一为陈留，以刚直几不免，犹滨于死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1173930_comment'></div>及复召，士大夫翕然向仰之，冀其且大用，然遂汩没不进，未能如其意、称其量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1173930_comment'></div>自以道终不行，而公长兄年九十矣，以太子宾客谢事家居，故求为留司官，以优游相从乡闾间，怡怡如也，有终焉之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1173930_comment'></div>呜呼，可谓笃于义，知所进退，不失其正者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1173930_comment'></div>性不妄悦人，虽穷困益坚，于时人鲜所合，而范文正公特知之，数荐于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1173930_comment'></div>其为政也，勇于当事，兴利若不及，去恶如恐失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1173930_comment'></div>亦以此故，仕尝难进易退，然其处之晏然，未尝以见色辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1173930_comment'></div>喜读书属文，尤长于为诗，诗凡千馀篇，读之其志可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1173930_comment'></div>夫人叶氏，封冯翊县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1173930_comment'></div>三子：长汉臣，进士及第，为长举令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1173930_comment'></div>次真臣，试将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1173930_comment'></div>皆能世其家者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1173930_comment'></div>次某尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1173930_comment'></div>三女：长适大理寺丞尚颖，次适秘书丞孙圭，其季未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1173930_comment'></div>某也，公之甥也，故于公之葬，得叙其志而铭其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1173930_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1173930'>为道者有言：白则涅矣，刚则缺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1173930_comment'></div>嗟嗟舅氏，涅而不变，缺而不卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1173930_comment'></div>硁硁其声，矫矫其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1173930_comment'></div>极晦而明，其辱则荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1173930_comment'></div>孰不公侯，孰不耄期？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1173930_comment'></div>人也天欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1173930_comment'></div>其止于斯！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1173930_comment'></div>我葬舅氏，悠悠我思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1173930_comment'></div>铭以藏之，以写我悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1173930_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月</a>　作《翰林学士吴君前夫人赵氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十三。当应吴奎之请而作。）</span><div id='poem_1173934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翰林学士吴君前夫人赵氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173934")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173934'>翰林学士吴君长文之元配赵夫人者，冀州信都人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173934_comment'></div>父立，仕为遂平令，家颇饶于财，怜其子，为择所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173934_comment'></div>至年二十，翰林君尚未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173934_comment'></div>治孔氏《书》、王氏《易》，通达有闻，而遂平贤之，以女予之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173934_comment'></div>夫人既归吴氏，事尊章迨及祖姑，婉嫕敏恪，执勤左右，夙夜不懈，虽退居其宫，未尝有惰色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173934_comment'></div>吴氏甚贫，夫人不敢有私财，自其所赍服玩器用百物者，茍可以备家费，缓急无所爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173934_comment'></div>以故族人无内外小大，皆归其贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173934_comment'></div>翰林以经明选于礼部，调为福州古田尉，广信军判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173934_comment'></div>夫人皆随以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173934_comment'></div>人谓其去舅姑之侧，当少暇豫自宽，而夫人滋益恭，犹其故时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173934_comment'></div>观其志，不为远近有所辍作，虽贤士大夫或不能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173934_comment'></div>宝元二年八月二十二日以疾终，年三十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173934_comment'></div>其后翰林以廉能升王朝，又举贤良，对策直言，天子用为谏臣，遂掌制命，召为学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173934_comment'></div>显贵得封其妻县郡君，而夫人不及封，人皆为之恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173934_comment'></div>夫人凡生一男二女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173934_comment'></div>男曰璟，有至性，其幼也，未能识其母，长而思慕悲哀，有过于人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173934_comment'></div>今补太庙室长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173934_comment'></div>长女嫁秘书省著作佐郎胡稷臣而亡，其次嫁泉州司法参军王孝宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173934_comment'></div>初，吴氏自齐之禹城徙北海，九世矣，由曾祖而下，稿肂未葬，翰林卜其地，得东阿之鱼山乡孟栅原为吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173934_comment'></div>嘉祐四年十月告于朝，迁曾祖妣王考以葬，而举夫人之丧以从，曰：「生不与我同其乐矣，死若有知也，其祔于祖姑，尚获其志焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173934_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1173934'>女得其归，妇宜其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173934_comment'></div>不幸不淑，悲如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173934_comment'></div>夫也茔之，子也承之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173934_comment'></div>祔于祖姑，万世其宁之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1173934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年11月</a>　十一月，与范镇同看详诸州编配罪人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年12月</a>　十二月，上《论让官疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论让官疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173615")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173615'>臣伏见故事，诸让官者，或一让，或再让，或三让，皆有品秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173615_comment'></div>非不欲人人让也，让之迹近名，近名则容伪，而为礼者恶烦，烦近于亵，故设中制，有所止之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173615_comment'></div>昔舜命九官，夔、龙不让，其他伯益之徒，一让而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173615_comment'></div>此则治世之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173615_comment'></div>窃见顷来士大夫，每有除命，不问高下，例辄累让，虽有出其至诚，恬于势利，然亦已逾典制，过夔、益矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173615_comment'></div>若习俗遂巧，流风稍敝，必且挟伪采名，要上迷众，更以为进取之捷径，奔竞之秘策，甚可恶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173615_comment'></div>岂独烦于礼哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173615_comment'></div>夫让虽美道，君子所有馀，小人所不足，然非其真，则丑亦甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173615_comment'></div>昔郑公孙段辞为卿，退则又使太史命己，子产恶其为人，其后卒为乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173615_comment'></div>故饰伪之敝至于此，非国家之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173615_comment'></div>公孙段尚其小者耳，子之擅燕，王莽代汉，其始皆以善自名，已而稍入于邪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173615_comment'></div>臣谓贤者之节，难进而易退者，非让一官之谓也，谓其能择于义，不犯非礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173615_comment'></div>故虽不多让，其节遒可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173615_comment'></div>众人之情，好得而恶失，好得而恶失者，亦非勉受一职之谓也，谓其不择于义，越礼而动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173615_comment'></div>故虽复饰让，其情亦弥险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173615_comment'></div>让与不让，一以故事旧典为准，无使钓利者要君，采名者售伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173615_comment'></div>不幸而不值子产之精识，则公孙段之徒，纷然竞于朝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173615_comment'></div>臣言似迂，而虑实远，望赐财择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1173615_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a><div id='poem_1173585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论孟阳河公事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173585")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173585'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173585'>臣伏见军巡院现勘孟阳河公事，准中书劄子，惟只取勘后来检计官吏壕寨等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173585_comment'></div>臣窃闻众议皆云，相度此河，本由杨佐，所役人夫七八千人，掘破丘墓百五十馀处，生者劳敝，死者暴露，百姓怨痛，谤议沸腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173585_comment'></div>今舍佐不问，专罪馀人，未审出于圣意，将由有司之误？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173585_comment'></div>以此断狱，恐不合人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173585_comment'></div>况自正月以来，和气不应，风雪为沴，人多死亡，未必非政役失中、刑罪乖当之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173585_comment'></div>臣忝司刑狱，既有所见，不敢不陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173585_comment'></div>其孟阳河公事，伏乞断自圣衷，以相度者为首，检计者为从，一例取勘，重行贬黜，少谢劳敝之众，粗慰暴露之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173585_comment'></div>且匹夫匹妇，精诚有以动天，伏望不以臣言为迂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173585_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1173585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　御史吴中复荐郑叔熊，刘敞讥之，遭吴中复等人谗言攻讦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　上《论睦亲宅不当建神御殿疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论睦亲宅不当建神御殿疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173582")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173582'>臣伏见古之正礼，诸侯不祖天子，公庙不可设于私家，所以明正统，尊一人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173582_comment'></div>今睦亲宅兴建神御殿，不合王制，不应经义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173582_comment'></div>窃闻圣慈，以天寒人劳，权罢役徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173582_comment'></div>臣谓若于礼当作，则不可以人劳之故而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173582_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173582_comment'></div>祖宗至尊也，役徒至贱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173582_comment'></div>恤至贱之众，而辍至尊之庙，非所以为名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173582_comment'></div>若礼本不当作，则不如遂止之耳，何以权罢哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173582_comment'></div>伏乞令礼官详议其事，使下不爽于名，上不愆于礼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1173582_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　上《论灾变宜使儒臣据经义以言疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论灾变宜使儒臣据经义以言疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173597")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173597'>臣伏以圣王所甚畏事者莫如天，所甚听用者莫如民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173597_comment'></div>是故观天意于灾祥，详民情于谣俗，因灾祥以求治之得失，原谣俗以知政之善否，诚少留意，则皆灿然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173597_comment'></div>前古贤圣之君，莫不循此以导其下，忠信之臣，莫不缘此以讽其上，上下相饬，而自天祐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173597_comment'></div>窃见朝廷每有吉应嘉瑞，则公卿称贺，至于灾异非常可怪之事，则寂然莫有言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173597_comment'></div>虽归美将顺，臣子之常操，而于戒儆吁俞，理似未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173597_comment'></div>陛下复不自延问，以求天意，恐非所谓「小心翼翼，昭事上帝，聿怀多福」者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173597_comment'></div>臣愚以为，五经灾异之说，最深最切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173597_comment'></div>凡四方所上奇物怪变、妖孽沴疾、有非常可疑者，宜使儒学之臣，据经义傅时事以言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173597_comment'></div>若其言是，可当天意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173597_comment'></div>若其言非，足以广圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173597_comment'></div>如近日雨雪骤寒，人有冻死者，此亦灾变之一端矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173597_comment'></div>惟聪明睿知，深思远虑，顺时谨微，不可不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173597_comment'></div>臣忝近列，愚不能通古今，窃观前世商高宗、周成王畏天威、享福祚之益，诚愿陛下留意于此，臣不胜区区。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1173597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　是年，作《出城》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　是年，作《杂咏》诗，自述发白齿脱。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷九。）</span><div id='poem_498026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杂咏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498026")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498026'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498026'>今年四十一，发白牙齿脱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498026'>未能游逍遥，意每不自豁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498026'>偶寻乐天诗，往在江州日。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498026'>年几与我同，哀疾与我埒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498026'>伊人了无生，外物均寂灭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498026'>而且于形骸，变化难自适。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498026'>况我狭中者，万缘日相伐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_498026'>力小觉任重，忧多使内热。<div id='poem_sentence_7_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_498026'>安能保平和，但有就衰竭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_498026'>贤哉香山翁，精诚妙前哲。<div id='poem_sentence_9_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_498026'>悬车未六十，鼓缶终大耋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_498026'>以兹揆损益，亦似有与夺。<div id='poem_sentence_11_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_498026'>至理何心得，吾其守兹说。<div id='poem_sentence_12_498026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_498026'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_498026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年1月</a>　正月，刁约知越州，刘敞作《送刁越州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十四。）</span><div id='poem_498901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刁越州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498901")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498901'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498901'>笑持符印下瀛州，真得千岩万壑游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498901'>父老为郎无自苦，鉴中行乐不知秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498901'>居人旧俗多姚姒，幕府连城半斗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498901'>太守会兼四千石，玺书宁复久淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498901'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498901_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年3月</a>　三月丁巳，上。作品：《论茶法疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《历代名臣奏议》卷二六四。）</span><div id='poem_1173637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论茶法疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐五年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173637")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173637'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173637'>臣伏以古人有言：「利不百，不变法」，盖言立事之难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173637_comment'></div>曩者朝廷变更茶法，诚欲便百姓阜国用而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173637_comment'></div>自变法以来，繇东南来者，更言其不便，徒以元敕不欲人立异，故一切缄默，莫敢正言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173637_comment'></div>其大要以谓先时百姓之摘山者，授钱于官，而今也顾使之纳钱于官，受纳之间，利害百倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173637_comment'></div>先时百姓冒法贩茶者被罚耳，今悉均赋于民，赋不时入，刑亦及之，是良民代冒法者受罪，子子孙孙未见其已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173637_comment'></div>先时大商富贾为国贸迁，而州郡收其税，今大商富贾不行，则税额不登，且乏国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173637_comment'></div>此三者最其害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173637_comment'></div>或以谓法遂不变，则中家必困，小家必流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173637_comment'></div>若因缘驱逼，起为盗贼，甚非国家之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173637_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞申敕有司，益采舆议，且收格前诏，极论可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173637_comment'></div>若朝廷能粲然复三代之遗风，捐山泽之末禁，则乞一弛茶利，恣民勿问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173637_comment'></div>设以为国用尚繁，利源未可悉除，犹当择其利害，变而通之，使公私两济，若求益反损，求利反害，臣恐东南六路数十州之民由此而困，则非所谓「利不百，不变法」者也，未知其可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173637_comment'></div>臣暗于时事，不足商功利，然耳之所闻，心之所疑，不敢不陈，望朝廷因臣言以求便国惠民之策而已，至于细意委曲，臣亦不能尽也。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1173637'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1173637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年4月</a>　是年四月，梅尧臣卒，作《同永叔哭圣俞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_498419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同永叔哭圣俞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498419")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498419'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498419'>子真之后千馀年，人物寥落无几传。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498419'>圣俞晚出江海壖，眉目自觉真神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498419'>气如阳秋和以妍，文若河汉清且渊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498419'>大钧匠物岂强镌，飞黄绝尘宁俟鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498419'>名为实宾道所捐，才与时逆行苦邅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498419'>起草建礼衰可怜，掌教国子寒无毡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498419'>谁不富贵君重迁，谁不耄期君疾蹎。<div id='poem_sentence_6_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_498419'>长松摧壑芝焚烟，谁其尸之当问天。<div id='poem_sentence_7_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_498419'>遗草大小三千篇，白玉落落珠联联。<div id='poem_sentence_8_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_498419'>此自可敌当世权，物莫两大犹信然。<div id='poem_sentence_9_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_498419'>我家江南再世前，与君通家情有连。<div id='poem_sentence_10_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_498419'>见君总角今华颠，于我莫逆好已偏。<div id='poem_sentence_11_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_498419'>今也已矣嗟绝弦，泪如翻波正沦涟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_498419'>翰林文章日月悬，凿石铭德埋九泉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_498419'>上书立后禄绍先，分宅恤穷祭有田。<div id='poem_sentence_14_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_498419'>呜呼岂非天下贤。<div id='poem_sentence_15_498419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_498419'>义不背死而苟焉，念子可以无悁悁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_498419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　是年四月，梅尧臣卒，作《圣俞挽词》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十二。）</span><div id='poem_498782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498782?labeling=true'
