"poem_title_498782")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498782'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498782'>孤宦众人后，空名三十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498782'>交游一时绝，诗笔四方传。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498782'>归旐江湖永，藏书日月边。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498782'>应封史通子，他日慰穷泉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498782'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498782'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_498782_0'>⑴ 自注：圣俞预修《唐书》，书成未上而亡。议者欲请于朝，赐一子官，以追宠之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498782_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年5月</a>　五月，好友江休复卒，作《邻几挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十二。）</span><div id='poem_498780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邻几挽词二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（其叔为之主）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498780")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498780'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498780'>那知一樽酒，流涕寝门前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498780'>非复平生日，空看东逝川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498780'>诗书遗素业，山水閟空弦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498780'>人物陈留古，当凭耆旧传。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498780'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498780_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_498781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498781?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年5月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498781'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498781'>忘年一倾盖，适意两虚舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498781'>老去翻相失，人生固若浮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498781'>萧条蒿里饯，零落竹林游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498781'>知与不知者，同时俱涕流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498781'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498781_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　五月，好友江休复卒，作《江休复祭文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十。）</span><div id='poem_1173954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江休复祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173954")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173954'>呜呼，当今之时，学不为人，仕不期通，养不耻贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173954_comment'></div>吾于邻几，独谓得之，何辜于天，而至于斯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173954_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173954_comment'></div>君始遘疾，物不甚治，固曰吾命，将有所制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173954_comment'></div>笑语作书，命子后事，其处寿夭，可谓不贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173954_comment'></div>某之得交，从蔡汝南，待我忘年，不耻不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173954_comment'></div>直谅多闻，所益者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173954_comment'></div>十有馀年，若青依蓝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173954_comment'></div>亦有出处，东西南北，意气之合，常若在侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173954_comment'></div>亦有毁誉，苍蝇红紫，议论之同，流言以止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173954_comment'></div>君今永归，使我从谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173954_comment'></div>伐木之感，悽其孔悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173954_comment'></div>酌酒陈肴，叙心以词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173954_comment'></div>平生之欢，从此而违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173954_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1173954_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年7月</a>　七月，题自书《秋水》篇。作品：《题自书〈秋水〉篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《清河书画舫》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1173786' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173786' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173786?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题自书秋水篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173786")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173786_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173786'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173786'>每读《南华》，至《秋水》篇，辄三复不能已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173786_comment'></div>因得圣从所遗蜀乌丝栏自书之，至「夔怜蚿」以下不录，聊取所赏适云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173786_comment'></div>嘉祐庚子秋七月廿九日刘敞原父题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1173786_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年7月</a>　七月，为杜惟则作墓志铭。作品：《故尚书虞部员外郎分司南京赠光禄卿杜君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故尚书虞部员外郎分司南京赠光禄卿杜君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐五年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173931")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173931'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173931'>君讳惟则，字定国，姓杜氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173931_comment'></div>其先蜀人，少举进士，不遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173931_comment'></div>而其兄以尚书郎守睦州，当先帝即位，四方贺受命，君亦奉其兄章，上礼有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173931_comment'></div>天子嘉之，召试学士院，得试秘书省校书郎，调含山县主簿，南雄州司理参军，稍迁德清江都令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173931_comment'></div>用荐者言，改大理寺丞，知南安县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173931_comment'></div>徙知雷州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173931_comment'></div>是时琼管有大狱，太守坐系者千八百人，吏民恫恐，上下莫自安，百姓废业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173931_comment'></div>而夷獠素易吏，狙伺重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173931_comment'></div>转运使患之，以狱事属君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173931_comment'></div>君帆海风，一日至郡下，条其情状，悉罢遣千七百馀人，而取其尤桀恶当坐者，具狱上廷尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173931_comment'></div>朝廷皆是之，吏民赖以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173931_comment'></div>改太子中舍、通判濠州，赐绯衣、银章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173931_comment'></div>又改殿中丞、通判杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173931_comment'></div>乾兴中，转国子博士、知处州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173931_comment'></div>迁尚书虞部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173931_comment'></div>年老，自表分司南京，因家于雍丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173931_comment'></div>君为人温厚和易，与人交，尚信义，久而益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173931_comment'></div>其言必践之，不为虚词以导悦人，亦未尝斥人过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173931_comment'></div>至于仕宦，视公事如私，视百姓如家人，茍可以便之，必商度处画，使得其宜而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173931_comment'></div>不求为名，故所至见爱，去之辄见思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173931_comment'></div>及其谢事归居也，乡里慕仰之，称为诚长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173931_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173931_comment'></div>考某，赠太仆卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173931_comment'></div>夫人某氏，封某县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173931_comment'></div>四子：长某早卒，次子某，次舜元，次叔元，三人者天圣八年同岁进士，而君夫人尚皆寿考无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173931_comment'></div>兄弟既成名，还家拜庆，一县往贺之，车马塞里巷，士大夫以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173931_comment'></div>君随其少子官淮阴，明年十一月某甲子卒，享年八十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173931_comment'></div>未及归葬，夫人、长子、次子、诸妇、诸孙相继又卒，贫不能自还，且三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173931_comment'></div>叔元乃克举君之丧，葬于某乡某原，而尽祔其馀，实嘉祐五年七月甲子云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173931_comment'></div>叔元固善士，孝慈有志节，自其宦于朝，数以令请赠君官，至光禄卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173931_comment'></div>然叔元之事亲，其设心以谓必己之所尽者，然后慊于义，是以其得反葬为艰且久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173931_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1173931'>以仕必才耶，致位一州，不为卑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173931_comment'></div>以寿必仁耶，至于耄期，不云微矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173931_comment'></div>嗟嗟杜君，乐易信厚，长者之规矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173931_comment'></div>实有良子，实收实食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173931_comment'></div>谓天不可信，于此乎视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173931_comment'></div>纳铭其丘，以诏后世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1173931_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年9月</a>　九月，除翰林侍读学士、知永兴军，上《谢加学士表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十四。）</span><div id='poem_1173643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173643")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173643'>常人之情，得所求而喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173643_comment'></div>智者之虑，过其任而忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173643_comment'></div>今边备虽严，帅责差易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173643_comment'></div>学者虽众，儒选实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173643_comment'></div>岂有贪就应声之求，忽忘非分之任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173643_comment'></div>怔忪失据，欣惧兼怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173643_comment'></div>固欲辞荣，不获承命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173643_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以薄技，起于诸生，内之无子产润色之才，外之无山甫将明之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173643_comment'></div>久典训诰，荐临藩垣，七年于兹，微效不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173643_comment'></div>犹以陪外廷之末，闻长者之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173643_comment'></div>间蒙分章，平议臣之奏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173643_comment'></div>时引大体，正宗庙之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173643_comment'></div>茍图纳忠，非敢忤物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173643_comment'></div>然而谗人饰词以巧诋，法吏挟怨以中伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173643_comment'></div>当是之时，几无以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173643_comment'></div>圣心先觉，公议尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173643_comment'></div>浸润之说不行，震惊之众为止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173643_comment'></div>风波可畏，天幸实多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173643_comment'></div>内私自怜，惧久得罪，辄丐千里之守，庶警一麾之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173643_comment'></div>不谓皇帝陛下，生成曲全，覆露无已，进增金华之讲，增重儒林之光，委以西州，适其素愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173643_comment'></div>望非所及，幸不可涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173643_comment'></div>夫匹夫一饭之恩，庸士然诺之信，犹能捐生出死，成功立名，况臣连数十城之封，兼四千石之重？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173643_comment'></div>于以宣明威信，抚养细民，尽其愚忠，庶无大悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173643_comment'></div>以此图报，敢为虚言？</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1173643'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1173643_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年10月</a>　十月，为皇室作十一篇墓志铭和十四篇石记。作品：为皇室作十一篇墓志铭和十四篇石记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年10月</a>　将赴扬州，上《论边臣劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十一。赴扬州原因不详，亦不知何据，疑《年谱》此处误以“永兴”为“扬州”）</span><div id='poem_1173586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论边臣劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173586")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173586'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173586'>臣伏以预备不虞，军之善政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173586_comment'></div>曩者元昊畔乱，西边震惊，骚动之患，延被天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173586_comment'></div>赖陛下神圣，与宗庙之灵，元昊殒灭，国内多故，其子幼弱，委政舅氏，故边鄙得以复安，百姓养老长幼，早寝宴起，此诚天道助善，中国之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173586_comment'></div>然自尔以来，又十馀年矣，其子益壮，窃谓虎狼野心，未可待以不疑，设使一旦发狂，能为风尘，而边备少懈，又如曩时，甚非豫虑制胜之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173586_comment'></div>臣望朝廷申敕边臣，常若寇至，城郭必固，甲兵必修，仓廪必实，赏罚必明，候望必谨，威信必立，使疆埸懔懔，无可乘之隙，则边患远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173586_comment'></div>顷者边吏颇以饮食之费、役使之佣得罪，即今武吏，多不愿临边，有不得已就职者，皆畏避微文，情不自聊，居常救过，苟免而已，缓急恐不足以责效，又非所以明朝廷大体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173586_comment'></div>孙沔、吕溱，皆贵重之臣，有功名于时，犹以此见废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173586_comment'></div>设复有孟舒、魏尚之徒，臣固知议者不能容之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173586_comment'></div>此乃冯唐所以疑汉文帝不能用廉颇、李牧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173586_comment'></div>乡饮酒之礼，一献百拜，其为修悫至矣，然而终不可以治军旅，则治军旅者，姑亦取其大节而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173586_comment'></div>边臣有材者寡，可用者少，臣愿陛下容养此辈，阔略细过，无甚督以微法，使得乐职嗜事，展力效用，人人思报上恩，则折冲远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173586_comment'></div>臣所部不当边剧，然而言此者，欲推明圣德，驾驭智勇之一端，非敢为边吏游说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173586_comment'></div>不胜区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173586_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1173586_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　作《论张茂实劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1173587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论张茂实劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173587")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173587'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173587'>臣伏以为国之道，防患于未然，远嫌于万一，所以安群情，止邪谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173587_comment'></div>伏闻张茂实，本周王乳母子，尝养宫中，故往年市人以狂言动茂实，颇骇物听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173587_comment'></div>近者韩绛又以谗说倾宰相，重摇人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173587_comment'></div>则是一茂实之身，远则为小人所指目，近则为群臣所疑惧，虽圣心坦然，于物无猜，恐未能家至户晓，使人人不惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173587_comment'></div>假令茂实其心如丹，必无他肠，亦未能家至户晓，使人人不忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173587_comment'></div>如此，则备宿卫、典兵马，适足以启天下之惑，动天下之忧，甚非重宗庙、安臣民、备万一之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173587_comment'></div>臣谓今日之宜，要令两善，莫若解茂实兵权，处以外郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173587_comment'></div>于茂实不失富贵，而朝廷得远嫌疑，此最策之善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173587_comment'></div>昔王郎自称刘子舆，卢芳自号刘文伯，因疑饰伪，未必皆有犯上之心，但流言驱扇，群情眩惑使之然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173587_comment'></div>臣忝近列，方当远出，心之所疑，不敢不极论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173587_comment'></div>乞以臣言，密付执政商量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173587_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1173587_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='497b9050f38a4a8491c529ae53c36084_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("497b9050f38a4a8491c529ae53c36084");'><span id='497b9050f38a4a8491c529ae53c36084_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1064')">1063-1064年</a>，45-46岁</div><div id='497b9050f38a4a8491c529ae53c36084' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年8月</a>　八月，召赴阙，勾当三班院，徙判太常寺，兼礼仪事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　为英宗进读《史记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　有诗《自陕到阙感而成咏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十三。）</span><div id='poem_498855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498855?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自陕到阙感而成咏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498855")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498855_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498855'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498855'>葱葱气象瞻峣阙，肃肃行装造近畿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498855'>钧奏昔年曾梦到，玉关今日是生归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498855'>茂林病久迷朝序，宣室人疏慑帝晖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498855'>簪履未忘恩再造，不然何路谒彤闱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498855'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498855_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年4月</a>　四月，刘敞得惊眩疾，求便郡养疾。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c0becc671bbc477aba5b1610ef4f18e1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c0becc671bbc477aba5b1610ef4f18e1");'><span id='c0becc671bbc477aba5b1610ef4f18e1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>，48岁</div><div id='c0becc671bbc477aba5b1610ef4f18e1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年11月</a>　在汴京，改官集贤院学士、权判南京留司御史台。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='84f5c7400d2142e9bee73b8106c133e4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("84f5c7400d2142e9bee73b8106c133e4");'><span id='84f5c7400d2142e9bee73b8106c133e4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>，21岁</div><div id='84f5c7400d2142e9bee73b8106c133e4' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在淮南，作《逐伯强文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三。嘉祐元年（1056）有《登扬州城北门予昔侍亲寓居此城下驿舍十八年矣怆然感动》，知此年刘敞随父刘立之寓居扬州。）</span><div id='poem_497684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_497684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/497684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>逐伯强文<span class='inlineComment2'>（鲍校作词并序）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_497684")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_497684_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_497684'>宝元二年，予羁旅淮南，医来言曰：今兹岁多疾疫。予因作文，以逐伯强。伯强，厉也，能为疫者，故逐也。</div><div id='poem_preface_497684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_497684'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_497684'>皇皇上天兮，浩浩后土。<div id='poem_sentence_0_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_497684'>厥生孔繁兮，其施甚溥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_497684'>陶陶仲夏兮，草木蕃庑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497684'>鸟兽孳息兮，我民乐胥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497684'>我民孔灵兮，上帝是仁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_497684'>天子孔圣兮，百工日新。<div id='poem_sentence_5_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_497684'>上无秕政兮，下无悖人。<div id='poem_sentence_6_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_497684'>邻里其集兮，乐哉欣欣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_497684'>伯强何为兮，孰畀以政。<div id='poem_sentence_8_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_497684'>反世五福兮，持极以令。<div id='poem_sentence_9_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_497684'>我民不怡兮，既丧其盛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_497684'>白黑眩瞀兮，孰察其正。<div id='poem_sentence_11_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_497684'>谓寿反天兮，谓康反病。<div id='poem_sentence_12_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_497684'>仁义无益兮，苟且为幸。<div id='poem_sentence_13_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_497684'>嗟尔子<span class='inlineComment2'>（刘本作伯，下同）</span>强兮，其独何心。<div id='poem_sentence_14_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_497684'>绝世和气兮，俾民不任。<div id='poem_sentence_15_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_497684'>上天孔神兮，大德曰生。<div id='poem_sentence_16_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_497684'>天不可长罔兮，民不可久侵。<div id='poem_sentence_17_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_497684'>天诛诚加兮靡所避，雷公驱兮风伯逝，嗟尔子强兮何所诣。<div id='poem_sentence_18_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_497684'>南有蛮兮，为寇为逋。<div id='poem_sentence_19_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_497684'>西羌戎兮，恃艰自虞。<div id='poem_sentence_20_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_497684'>天子孔仁兮，靡焉毕屠。<div id='poem_sentence_21_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_497684'>子强往兮，代天伐诛。<div id='poem_sentence_22_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_497684'>嗟中国兮，不可久留。<div id='poem_sentence_23_497684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_497684'>子不去兮，颠倒思予。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_497684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在淮南，作《送刘初平序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十五。嘉祐元年（1056）有《登扬州城北门予昔侍亲寓居此城下驿舍十八年矣怆然感动》，知此年刘敞随父刘立之寓居扬州。）</span><div id='poem_1173766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173766?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刘初平序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173766")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173766_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173766'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173766'>读书而讲道，据权而涖事，其功德易以及民，孰若士大夫耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173766_comment'></div>然而天下緤组垂绂、爵上闻者，无不慕山林之士，而愿与之齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173766_comment'></div>为山林者，嚣然若固当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173766_comment'></div>此其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173766_comment'></div>岂朝廷之士真可薄，山林之士真可高？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173766_comment'></div>彼何予之而不辞，此何受之而不让乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173766_comment'></div>亦曰不污于利，不近于耻，不亲于忧，不烦于事，苟异乎此者，无不慕焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173766_comment'></div>如此，虽糠秕乎尧舜，无非者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173766_comment'></div>若刘生者，岂真士大夫所慕者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173766_comment'></div>其游遍公卿，无往而不若旧相识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173766_comment'></div>使污于利，近于耻，亲于忧，烦于事，而能尔乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173766_comment'></div>往者朝廷喜求才，拔草野，有出茅屋任谏大夫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173766_comment'></div>后太平，益厌懈，人亦益近薄，故蒲草圭璧，往往流于瞽叟，而诏书亦辄以先生处士宠之，欲以致后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173766_comment'></div>今刘君好史书，语当世事有权变，又博识多前知，为士大大所称，而未闻有以举应诏者，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173766_comment'></div>事固有难知者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173766_comment'></div>行矣，入于越，诚将见范公，愿以告曰：「斯道也，将亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173766_comment'></div>茍相天下也，而能勿兴此乎」？</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1173766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在淮南，作《送刘初平谒会稽范吏部》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集 》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷九。嘉祐元年（1057）有《登扬州城北门予昔侍亲寓居此城下驿舍十八年矣怆然感动》，知此年刘敞随父刘立之寓居扬州。年谱未提及此诗，但据诗中内容来看与《送刘初平序》吻合，应是作于同时。）</span><div id='poem_498017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刘初平谒会稽范吏部</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498017")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498017'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498017'>刘生大梁客，五十耻独醒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498017'>观书泛为通，不肯明一经。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498017'>壮岁怀慷慨，边游忍伶仃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498017'>担簦售白璧，垂蒯提青萍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498017'>归来面朝士，口写山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>川形。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498017'>公侯尽高意，礼数争分庭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498017'>落魄破小节，浮游谢尘冥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_498017'>诙谐若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_498017", 498017, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>流輠</span>，捷胜如建瓴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_498017'>荏苒混朝市，缤纷迈年龄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_498017'>有云致官爵，百说无一听。<div id='poem_sentence_9_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_498017'>二子才剑吷，众豪固螟蛉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_498017'>以兹滞玉帛，亦不羞岩坰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_498017'>太尉辟开府<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：夏竦也。）</span>，中丞请居廷<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：孔道辅也。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_498017'>拂衣东南走，高揖千岩青。<div id='poem_sentence_13_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_498017'>禹穴发穷宝，雷门叩惊霆。<div id='poem_sentence_14_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_498017'>邦侯万人杰，忧国心无宁。<div id='poem_sentence_15_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_498017'>得善辄解榻，发奇肖开硎。<div id='poem_sentence_16_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_498017'>抽辞肯听莹，宴旧方淹停。<div id='poem_sentence_17_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_498017'>箬下进醇酎，鉴中结飞铃。<div id='poem_sentence_18_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_498017'>高哉鸿鹄心，去矣穷沧溟。<div id='poem_sentence_19_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_498017'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_498017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498017'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_498017_0'>⑴ 原作出，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498017_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ab1e02e519c54c0f8d8097ba8929bce8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab1e02e519c54c0f8d8097ba8929bce8");'><span id='ab1e02e519c54c0f8d8097ba8929bce8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，38岁</div><div id='ab1e02e519c54c0f8d8097ba8929bce8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　至扬州，作《扬州谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十四。）</span><div id='poem_1173641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173641?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173641")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173641'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173641'>一介之材，善无所取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173641_comment'></div>千里之地，任为不轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173641_comment'></div>仰戴恩华，退增惭惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173641_comment'></div>臣闻事上之行，莫若爱君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173641_comment'></div>爱君之臣，莫重去国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173641_comment'></div>汲黯遗言李息，望之致意本朝，古今美谈，贤哲馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173641_comment'></div>况臣本以薄技，遘兹昌辰，幸得出入周卫之中，优游侍从之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173641_comment'></div>持橐簪笔，庶乎寡尤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173641_comment'></div>带剑佩衡，足以自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173641_comment'></div>岂其轻去严密之奉，偷得便安之私？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173641_comment'></div>盖引嫌避亲，中外著令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173641_comment'></div>因事补吏，朝廷通规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173641_comment'></div>幸蒙赐可之事，殆殊共治之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173641_comment'></div>伏遇皇帝陛下，天度容物，圣资尽人，揆其忠诚，非有违象魏之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173641_comment'></div>察其浅识，犹足寄民社之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173641_comment'></div>沛然德音，委以符竹，敢不勤恤人隐，奉宣上恩，自饬固陋之心，庶几乐易之政。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1173641_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　作《扬州到任谢上启》，在扬州，以宽简治民，还民雷塘田。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十五。）</span><div id='poem_1173728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州到任谢上启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173728")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173728'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173728'>右，某启：朝廷欲治，未尝轻长人之权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173728_comment'></div>郡国甚微，亦皆有分土之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173728_comment'></div>然则宜得智力肃给，器能周通，上足以奉宣诏恩，下可以表率方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173728_comment'></div>岂伊浅薄，辄误简求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173728_comment'></div>伏惟某官，登翊圣期，恢张王纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173728_comment'></div>乐育人物，因材而措之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173728_comment'></div>熙成天工，授方而效以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173728_comment'></div>将使懦质，有资昌时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173728_comment'></div>昔汲黯之忠，不难淮阳，而眷眷于李息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173728_comment'></div>萧侯之节，非疏平原，而汲汲于本朝<span class='inlineComment2'>（下缺。《公是集》卷四五。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1173728'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1173728_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　作《雷陂劝耕作杂言》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷十七。）</span><div id='poem_498377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雷陂劝耕作杂言<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498377")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498377_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_498377_0'>① 此陂盖江都宫之地，吴王钓台在其旁。先时民三十家耕其中，后强为吏所夺，废不耕者十馀年矣。子按地籍，悉召还耕者，使县大夫授之地，如其旧</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498377'>君不见江都宫，昔时何崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498377'>下临雷陂水，前踞吴王台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498377'>台倾无馀级，水竭空尘埃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498377'>隋人已曾顾此长叹息，今世更为隋人哀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498377'>乃知天地间，一盛亦一衰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498377'>但从伏羲已来三十馀万岁，未有书契胜言哉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498377'>尧桀是非可<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>两忘，我欲劝人辟草莱。<div id='poem_sentence_6_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_498377'>种稻水一方，艺麻陵<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>四颓。<div id='poem_sentence_7_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_498377'>爽鸠之乐非我有，聊独玩此田莓莓。<div id='poem_sentence_8_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_498377'>未知百世<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>间，更复谁当来。<div id='poem_sentence_9_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_498377'>且欲及閒从宾客，省耕访此时徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_498377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_498377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498377'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_498377_0'>⑴ 原作何，据名贤本、明抄本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_498377_0'>⑵ 名贤本、傅校作塍</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_498377_0'>⑶ 名贤本、明抄本作年</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498377_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　上《请罢五溪之征疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢五溪之征疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173609")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173609'>臣闻舜为天子，禹为司空，伯益赞之，君臣之盛自古未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173609_comment'></div>以伐三苗，曾不得咫尺之地，因班师振旅而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173609_comment'></div>晋郤缺率诸侯之师八百馀乘，挟公子捷菑以攻邾娄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173609_comment'></div>斥堠不设，城门不闭，以韦帛通语言，诸侯皆罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173609_comment'></div>故曰：「非吾力不能攻，义实不尔克也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173609_comment'></div>此二者皆不可谓善战矣，然舜禹不以其故贬圣，伯益、郤缺不以其故损贤，理有逆顺，义有曲直也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173609_comment'></div>今武溪诸彭，父子结怨，而边臣轻发兵，为子讨父，得无非春秋王霸之略乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173609_comment'></div>臣以谓过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173609_comment'></div>智者欲骋其巧，勇者欲用其力，矫箭累弦，励剑负戟，以深入为事，甚非治天下之大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173609_comment'></div>臣闻古者三王之伐，征不贡，讨不朝，今彭氏父子所以争一旦之命者，乃自失职，不得朝贡也，臣以谓可听以休边民，此舜禹之策，益、郤之义，所以明于典谟《春秋》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173609_comment'></div>往年岁星在鹑尾，则宜厚仁义以应之，而始诛五溪，逆父子之节，难以得天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173609_comment'></div>今盛夏动众，下潦上雾，多毒蛇恶草之害，难以得地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173609_comment'></div>得天地之道者，自古五帝三王之所以务通而顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173609_comment'></div>虽有圣辩，莫之能变其说，而况纵欲贪功，徼一时之胜者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173609_comment'></div>恐此为人臣之利，而非国家之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173609_comment'></div>臣愿朝廷谨之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1173609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年9月</a>　九月，改元嘉祐，进朝散大夫，封宣县开国男。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在扬州时，举荐孙侔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　在扬州时，作《扬州赛庙文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十。）</span><div id='poem_1173977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州赛庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173977")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173977'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173977'>年月日，某官某，谨以清酌庶羞，祭于城隍之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173977_comment'></div>乃十二月晦，某以自冬无雪，愆阳为灾，大恐害岁事，以乏上下之祀，用乞灵于尔有神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173977_comment'></div>惟尔有神，实鉴厥衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173977_comment'></div>其夕雨雪，若响之答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173977_comment'></div>益之以霢霂，既优既渥，既沾既足，小大欣欣，罔不逸豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173977_comment'></div>谨择良日，荐此苾芬，以报灵德，示人不欺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1173977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年11月</a>　十一月甲子，舅王冲以疾终。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='48afc222a50b48728f11847d3bef0020_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("48afc222a50b48728f11847d3bef0020");'><span id='48afc222a50b48728f11847d3bef0020_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1058')">1056-1058年</a>，38-40岁</div><div id='48afc222a50b48728f11847d3bef0020' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　是年，与杜衍相识，是时，杜衍已致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　是年，作《登扬州城北门予昔侍亲寓居此城下驿舍十八年矣怆然感动》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十一。）</span><div id='poem_498705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登扬州城北门予昔侍亲寓居此城下驿舍十八年矣怆然感动</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498705")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498705'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498705'>昔钓城下水，今来十八年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498705'>居人几能在，里巷独依然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498705'>手种成乔木，躬耕有废田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498705'>悲歌顾千骑，不觉涕沦涟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498705'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498705_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年5月</a>　五月，作《乞置狱官奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《续资治通鉴长编》卷一八五。）</span><div id='poem_1173628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173628?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞置狱官奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173628")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173628_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173628'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173628'>臣伏闻朝廷选官删定殿前、马、步军等司编敕条贯，诚为要务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173628_comment'></div>臣以谓科律虽详，执而用之者吏也，若不审，则狱容有滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173628_comment'></div>今殿前等司所以统诸军，刑罚不少，而鞫讯论决一委胥吏，曾无掾曹士大夫参其閒，即有猾吏因事侮文，其势不难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173628_comment'></div>狱者重事，人命所系，自古以来，未尝独任小吏，不关搢绅者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173628_comment'></div>又汉、唐大将军营卫幕府，或设军政议郎、录事、兵曹、分职联事，其员甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173628_comment'></div>今诚制度太简略，欲尽如古难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173628_comment'></div>且每司置狱官一员，专典鞫狱，令流内铨选补，如左右军巡判官例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173628_comment'></div>如此，狱可使不冤，刑可使不误，庶几上副朝廷钦恤之意，愈于专修编敕而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1173628_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　郭恩战死，刘敞作《丁酉五月郭守恩战殁武戡走入壁守恩勇将有智略》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十二。）</span><div id='poem_498771' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498771' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498771?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁酉五月郭守恩战殁武戡走入壁守恩勇将有智略</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498771")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498771_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498771'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498771'>敌兵得汉巧，五月战西河。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498771'>壮士平原死，孤城杀气多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498771'>犹闻疏勒守，无复鲁阳戈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498771'>不反东流水，滔滔奈尔何。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498771'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498771_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年12月</a>　十二月，上《请诸州各辟教官疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请诸州各辟教官疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173600")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173600'>臣伏见近敕，更张贡举条约，欲令四方游士，各归其乡里，而有司得以观行听言，绝滥进之弊，此诚上近古制，下适时宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173600_comment'></div>然臣犹谓必欲人安其居，皆有常心，渐之于仁，摩之于义，化民成俗，则莫若开庠序以收养之，设师弟子以教诲之，月考时试以劝勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173600_comment'></div>教定俗成，然后贤不肖立见，而真伪不杂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173600_comment'></div>今州郡皆有学，学皆有生徒，而终患无师以教之，但令掾曹领其事，职既不专，教用不明，自古儒学之官不兼治民，盖为此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173600_comment'></div>臣欲乞州郡有学处，听长史各奏辟教授一员，于前任判司簿尉中，选有文行、堪为人师者充，仍令以四年为一任，学理考数、官资俸禄同之掾曹，则学有常师，教有常业，士子竞劝矣，于朝廷长育人材之意，诚未失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173600_comment'></div>今欲游士归乡，而不为设学，则无以收之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173600_comment'></div>设学而不为置师，则无以率之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173600_comment'></div>置师而不立课试讲习之法，则无以成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173600_comment'></div>三者名存实亡，则学者不归，虽欲别贤不肖，兴廉让，崇乡党之化，不可得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173600_comment'></div>惟陛下裁许。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1173600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年12月</a>　十二月，作《时会堂诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十四。）</span><div id='poem_1173778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>时会堂诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173778")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173778'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173778'>州城北带广阜，古所谓昆崙冈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173778_comment'></div>其木宜茶，与蒙顶比，故或谓之蜀冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173778_comment'></div>太守岁贡蜀冈茶，以火前采之，发轻使驰至京师，不过十日，为天下先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173778_comment'></div>自禹抑洪水，分九牧，淮海惟扬州，其任土之法，若瑶琨、金木、筱簜、齿革、羽毛、织贝诸奇物，当备输王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173778_comment'></div>天子为其远费民力，皆止不以为常贡，常贡独茶，至简易矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173778_comment'></div>然犹岁所上不过三数斤，所以御于至尊者，贵精不贵衍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173778_comment'></div>世或说蒙顶茶宜久服，能轻身、除疾、却老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173778_comment'></div>诚有是者，岂非臣子所愿哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173778_comment'></div>《狸首》之诗，以时会为乐者，固诸侯之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173778_comment'></div>于是筑堂蜀江之阳，命曰时会，将率官属修职贡于此焉，且使来者世世勿忘服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173778_comment'></div>嘉祐二年十二月，右正言、知制诰、知扬州军州事刘某题辞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1173778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年12月</a>　十二月，《时会堂诗二首》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　是年，有《李觏以太学助教召曾巩以进士及第归俱会郡下素闻两人之贤留饮涵虚阁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_498198' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498198' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498198?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李觏以太学助教召曾巩以进士及第归俱会郡下素闻两人之贤留饮涵虚阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498198")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498198_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498198'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498198'>孤鸾方北游，威凤复南翔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498198'>邂逅中道遇，其<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>音何锵锵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498198'>太平向百年，此固多美祥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498198'>扰扰都人士，争先觌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>辉光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498198'>虽无醴泉流，江水清且长。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498198'>虽无朝阳桐，翠树茂且芳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498198'>念将万里逝，愿得少徬徨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_498198'>为君赋卷阿，因以谢楚狂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_498198'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_498198_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498198'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_498198_0'>⑴ 名贤本作弄，诗存本、明抄本作孔</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_498198_0'>⑵ 原作显，据名贤本、明抄本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498198_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　作《杜祁公挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十二。）</span><div id='poem_498730' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498730' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498730?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杜祁公挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498730")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498730_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498730'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498730'>天下苍生望，朝端百辟师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498730'>辞荣如弃躧，得道去乘箕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498730'>无复临雍问，空馀罢市悲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498730'>会书廊庙语，世世奉萧规。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498730'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498730_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_498731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498731?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498731'>第五廉莫比，留侯功不居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498731'>遗风何峻极，雅尚得冲虚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498731'>平昔常开阁，深惭晚曳裾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498731'>千金论一字，永慨袖中书<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498731'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_498731_0'>⑴ 自注：某去年方与公相识，后累得公书，皆草书亲笔，劲媚可爱。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498731_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　是年，长子刘定国亡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年1月</a>　正月，作《伯父宝书阁记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十六。）</span><div id='poem_1173886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伯父宝书阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173886")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173886'>初，伯父以尚书郎致政归，筑室于苏之长洲，曰：「吾昔为之宰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173886_comment'></div>赋役吾未尝不均也，因其力而时使之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173886_comment'></div>狱讼吾未尝不谨也，察其情而恕思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173886_comment'></div>人皆思我，后世居之安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173886_comment'></div>室既成，聚书数千卷，覆以重阁，指之示子孙曰：「此先帝以赐先子者也，此先子所以教后嗣者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173886_comment'></div>吾尝以此事亲，以此事君矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173886_comment'></div>行年八十，无悔于心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173886_comment'></div>今以遗汝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173886_comment'></div>吴中士大夫闻若言，皆记以为惇史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173886_comment'></div>某以为古之君子，莫难于择所处，择所处而当，故令闻长世，其身休焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173886_comment'></div>伯父之卜居也，于人之我思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173886_comment'></div>其遗子孙也，以己之事亲与君，而归于无悔心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173886_comment'></div>忠信学问而已矣，牛羊、仓廪、金玉之富不预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173886_comment'></div>《颂》不云乎：「在彼无恶，在此无斁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173886_comment'></div>虽庞氏之义，何以远过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173886_comment'></div>于是名其阁曰宝书阁，而刻其语于石，使后生有述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173886_comment'></div>若夫栋宇之制，奢约之度，智者可以观其则，仁者可以见其志，非为者所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173886_comment'></div>嘉祐三年正月，右正言、知制诰、知扬州军州事某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1173886_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年2月</a>　二月，沈康知常州，刘敞作《送沈康学士知常州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十四。）</span><div id='poem_498898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送沈康学士知常州<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498898")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498898_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_498898_0'>① 沈自博士除郡，某少时居客此州甚久</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498898'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498898'>三科妙选汉台臣，君去分符牧远人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498898'>富贵须为千骑长，中和好布万家春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498898'>山川阳羡由来胜，谣俗延陵自古淳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498898'>曾是倦游羁旅地，送行增<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作曾）</span>羡两朱轮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498898'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年4月</a>　四月，迁起居舍人、知郓州兼京东西路安抚使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a25a1d02fdda454d83b33f98c1e0f00c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a25a1d02fdda454d83b33f98c1e0f00c");'><span id='a25a1d02fdda454d83b33f98c1e0f00c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1041')">1040-1041年</a>，22-23岁</div><div id='a25a1d02fdda454d83b33f98c1e0f00c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年5月12日</a>　五月十二日，母王氏卒，父刘立之除服，寄居毗陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　是年作《谕客》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十八。）</span><div id='poem_1173873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谕客</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173873")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173873'>宝元、康定之间，元昊畔，诏书求才谋之士，于是言事自荐者甚众，辄下近臣问状，高者除部从事，其次补掾史，且数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173873_comment'></div>时予方游吴中，客有相哀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173873_comment'></div>作《谕客》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173873_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1173873'>客谓公是先生曰：「盖闻贤者不遗利，智者不失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173873_comment'></div>因形推势，以事为机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173873_comment'></div>是以功勋流于竹帛，盛德载于黎庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173873_comment'></div>历百世而不衰，掩众人以独骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173873_comment'></div>此所谓豪杰之士也，而先生亦有意于此乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173873_comment'></div>先生曰：「何以教之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173873_comment'></div>客曰：「今西兵距境，昆崙道绝，主上不怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173873_comment'></div>边有宿甲，旃裘之贡不入，钟鼓之娱不欢者，于今三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173873_comment'></div>是以下求贤之诏，开自荐之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173873_comment'></div>总揽奇俊，兼听天下，恩涵于人心，义激于肺腑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173873_comment'></div>故令下之日，坐者泣沾襟，卧者涕交颐，咸欲奋必死之力，蹈难测之机，忘山川之苦，薄战伐之危，请长缨以系颈，输家财以济师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173873_comment'></div>拜章者交乎公车，献策者满乎北阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173873_comment'></div>起徒步以析爵，由一言以改列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173873_comment'></div>此亦遭遇之时，变化之契，勇辩之辰，敌国之势，穰苴所以权军而西出，苏秦所以掉舌而东逝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173873_comment'></div>今先生乃悄乎如不知，藐乎如不闻，名与智寂，迹与世沦，怀书满腹，不如众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173873_comment'></div>意者，暗于事势而然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173873_comment'></div>且夫道期于用，不必全洁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173873_comment'></div>功期于成，不必无辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173873_comment'></div>是以伊尹负鼎，伍员鼓腹，百里食牛，包胥恸哭，乘时因势，大直细曲，崇如丘山，炳若执烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173873_comment'></div>今先生乃独习无用之言，守难行之事，遗弃诸子，专愚六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173873_comment'></div>井田虽通，不可以厚财赋之入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173873_comment'></div>乡饮虽讲，不可以助军旅之急；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173873_comment'></div>羽舞虽文，不可以代干戟之执；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173873_comment'></div>麻冕虽纯，不可以更甲胄之袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173873_comment'></div>雎盱拳曲，空言少实，不可图进取之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173873_comment'></div>则何不卑论侪俗，夜寝夙兴，驰骋乎孙、吴之场，揣摩乎苏、张之营，舌如电流，功如雷行，威名并建，家国两荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173873_comment'></div>乃反侈陋巷之处，甘藜藿之食，目无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1173873", 1173873, "Clauses/102/Comments/0")'>韶曼</span>，耳绝金石，抱瓮而汲，不知用力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173873_comment'></div>行身若此，老且奚益」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173873_comment'></div>先生曰：「吁，客何貌之壮而语之少，何愿之大而智之小？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173873_comment'></div>信难以议道矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173873_comment'></div>虽然，不可以不陈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173873_comment'></div>昔者轩辕有阪泉之师，尧有丹浦之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173873_comment'></div>舜有三苗之诛，启有扈氏之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173873_comment'></div>成汤造攻于牧宫，文王收绩于崇城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173873_comment'></div>当此之时，覆载侔于天地，文明比于日月，休恩渗于时雨，厉威粲于霜雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173873_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1173873", 1173873, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>跂行喙息</span>，罔有不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173873_comment'></div>然且弓矢未尽闭，干戈未尽戢，小至俘馘，大至流血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1173873_comment'></div>巍巍之功不为之差减，赫赫之号不为之灭裂，适足以增其徽名，广其休烈而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1173873_comment'></div>客以谓有损于盛德耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1173873_comment'></div>夫狂童鸱张，天夺其魄，跳踉颠豗，假使顷刻，亲戚不辅，鬼神所殛，狗吠其主，鼠窃疆埸，此与蚩尤、三苗何以异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1173873_comment'></div>然而将帅之臣阅于诗礼，介胄之卒奋于䝙兕，赏未及悬，刑未及峻，而天下之民，亿兆之众，固已集矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1173873_comment'></div>于是乎虎盼鹰视，龙行云起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1173873_comment'></div>譬如挽千石之弩，决垂溃之疽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1173873_comment'></div>引洪河之流，沃殆灭之燬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1173873_comment'></div>曾不移息而可见，又何足烦天下之学士？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1173873_comment'></div>主上所以朝乾夕惕，劳于求贤，通自进之路，开博访之门者，恐伯高、傅说之流藏于岩野，伊尹、太师之品逸于屠钓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1173873_comment'></div>又所以明谦让之义，恭听卑之操，使非常之业与士大夫共有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1173873_comment'></div>此乃三王所不及，五帝所难行，愚陋之人岂能昭见其情哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1173873_comment'></div>昔燕欲骏马，乃市朽骨，而千里之驹果至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1173873_comment'></div>越欲勇士，乃揖怒蛙，而百夫之勇来萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1173873_comment'></div>主上亦欲得特达之人，是以狂狷者无所咈，排触者无所忌，高爵重禄，或富或贵，鉴洞乎神明，量配乎天地，岂可以为小丑之未夷，群凶之尚恣哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1173873_comment'></div>且夫东渐岛夷，南及交趾，西奄孤竹，北越凿齿，受令朝朔，齐一车轨，雷动风行，方百万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1173873_comment'></div>观数郡之地，元昊之众，曾不若黑子之著，而蝼蚁之循穴，而欲以敌国论之，固失类矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1173873_comment'></div>且客独不闻宋受命之说乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1173873_comment'></div>昔者唐失其御，海水横溢，寰宇之内，分为六七，不贡不朝，靡所统一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1173873_comment'></div>于是蠢蠢之氓，困于戈鋋，积尸为山，流血为川，糜溃屠剥者，盖五十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1173873_comment'></div>上帝眷之，乃命太祖，受禅启国，方行千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1173873_comment'></div>犹有残孽，弗率弗祀，太宗平之，真宗成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1173873_comment'></div>至于制作之道，似或未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1173873_comment'></div>然亦开籍田，封泰山，礼河汾，考百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1173873_comment'></div>皇上率循圣武，靡有遗轶，而胜残去杀，适底今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1173873_comment'></div>是以往者申访古乐，绪正郊配，大定六籍，谨敕元会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1173873_comment'></div>欲以就一王之法，成必世之期，使后嗣遵其矩，太常肄其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1173873_comment'></div>参于六经，表于万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1173873_comment'></div>泽漏乎重溟，功陟乎上天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1173873_comment'></div>还成康之俗，俨典谟之篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1173873_comment'></div>包弓偃革，无得踰焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1173873_comment'></div>此学者所以踊跃，而鄙儒所以拳拳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1173873_comment'></div>何以誇苏、张于平世，侈孙、吴于异类？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1173873_comment'></div>终无益于王道，空自绝于圣治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1173873_comment'></div>客徒笑我暗于事机，我亦悲客躁于富贵，而不知制作之义也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1173873_comment'></div>言未毕，客竦然而谢曰：「荒野之人，溺于所闻，先生幸教之，谨受令矣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1173873_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1173873'>客：原脱，据鲍本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_75_1173873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1173873'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_74_1173873_1'>⑴ 《公是集》卷四八。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷一二八，《文翰类选大成》卷一四七，同治《新喻县志》卷一四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1173873_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年8月</a>　八月陕西经略安抚副使范仲淹兼知延州，敞作《贺龙图兼知延州》作品：《贺龙图兼知延安》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五。）</span><div id='poem_497832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_497832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/497832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺范龙图兼知延安</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_497832")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_497832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_497832'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_497832'>大兵昔摧伤，两将折旗鼓<span class='inlineComment2'>（傅校作辱狂虏）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_497832'>哀哉中国士，化作城下土。<div id='poem_sentence_1_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_497832'>冤魂不得返，杀气凌彼苍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497832'>天亦为之悲，白昼日无光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497832'>人言此城下，往往鬼神哭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_497832'>此事天子忧，此心大夫辱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_497832'>昔公守东越，人怨公不用。<div id='poem_sentence_6_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_497832'>今日公在西，知公德持重。<div id='poem_sentence_7_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_497832'>筑城不必坚，解甲不可攻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_497832'>何况保金城，弛张皆系公。<div id='poem_sentence_9_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_497832'>汲黯辅炎汉，淮南内竦惧。<div id='poem_sentence_10_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_497832'>郅都守穷边，匈奴为之去。<div id='poem_sentence_11_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_497832'>此事昔所闻，今日见所亲。<div id='poem_sentence_12_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_497832'>折冲樽俎间，震动旃裘民。<div id='poem_sentence_13_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_497832'>国耻行且刷，寇雠不可保。<div id='poem_sentence_14_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_497832'>斯人叹微管，愿及太平老。<div id='poem_sentence_15_497832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_497832'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_497832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　是年，长子定国生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　次子奉世生。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
汝南
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a71479adae9c4c4b860c91a4cc290d72_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a71479adae9c4c4b860c91a4cc290d72");'><span id='a71479adae9c4c4b860c91a4cc290d72_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1048')">1047-1048年</a>，29-30岁</div><div id='a71479adae9c4c4b860c91a4cc290d72' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　通判蔡州，与知州吴育相处甚欢，并初显其政治才能。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　上《论折变当随土地之宜疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论折变当随土地之宜疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173604")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173604'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173604'>臣闻圣王之处民也顺其性，是故居山者不使居川，居渚者不使居中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173604_comment'></div>其取民也任其宜，是故山虞不以鱼鳖为赋，川衡不以材木为贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173604_comment'></div>盖顺其性者，知天者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173604_comment'></div>任其宜者，知地者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173604_comment'></div>圣王之功不变天地，是以其养易足，其教易成，其求易贡，其取不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173604_comment'></div>今之时善言政者，莫不欲富民，欲富民而常患夺其财者，由有司取之反其性而戾其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173604_comment'></div>于是或以谷为金，或以刍为帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173604_comment'></div>粺非精也，而求之不舍，民是以困穷，是以流亡，是以盗争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173604_comment'></div>朝廷岂不恤哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173604_comment'></div>盖不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173604_comment'></div>臣以为方今用度不足之时，欲尽如古，盖亦不可，且敕有司，毋责鱼鳖于山，毋索材木于川，则百姓亦庶几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173604_comment'></div>臣非敢虚言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173604_comment'></div>臣所治州十县，其五皆种穜稑，而有司乃使以糯与粳为赋，一不如约，吏当坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173604_comment'></div>若此者，上则不顺于天，下则不因于地，中则不悦于人，去圣王之功远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173604_comment'></div>惟陛下哀怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173604_comment'></div>臣幸备职事，以治民为职，诏书问可以宽民者，臣窃疑莫先于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173604_comment'></div>夫赋税固自古有之，臣愿敕诸转运使，必不得已而变折其所有，毋变其所无；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173604_comment'></div>变其所可得，毋变其所不可得，则民疾不困矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1173604_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　有《鼓角楼宴集》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十四。）</span><div id='poem_498874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鼓角楼宴集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498874")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498874'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498874'>周城百雉拥中军，阿阁三间丽白云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498874'>燕雀总<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>知依盛德，山河相与助雄文<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：此楼府公作，自为之记。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498874'>轻裘缓带居多暇，旨酒嘉肴客易醺。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498874'>还识魏牟怀北醺，正逢长日扇南熏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498874'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_title_498897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498897'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498897'>南极微阳中夜新，碧池风物晓来春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498897'>鼓鼙似动鱼龙伏，旌旆不惊鸥鹭驯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_498972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498972'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498972'>斗城烟雾隔金銮，日破轻阴玉滴寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498972'>捷笔补天凌造化，高文惊世涌波澜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498972'>梦成白凤飞鸣远，功就丹梯步武宽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498972'>回首蓬莱笑清浅，春风前后发芝兰。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年闰1月</a>　通判蔡州，闰正月作《闰月朔日寄府公给事二首》，<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十。）</span><div id='poem_498562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_498562'>良闰百年逢<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：自周广顺至今，再闰正月。）</span>，佳辰献岁同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1173967_comment'></div>不敢忘德，恭荐苾芬，以答灵贶，以兴嗣岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173967_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1173967_comment'></div></div></div><br class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷九。益州路转运司设于益州（仁宗嘉祐四年1059升益州为成都府，益州路改成都府路），刘立之应是卒于益州，刘敞赴蜀迎灵柩亦因在益州。）</span><div id='poem_498044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498044' class='poemTitle -----title
密云
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1a04727ff5eb4c96afb6d616925baaee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1a04727ff5eb4c96afb6d616925baaee");'><span id='1a04727ff5eb4c96afb6d616925baaee_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奉使契丹途中过古北口，有《古北口》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十八。诗题下自注：“自古北口即奚人地，皆山居谷汲，耕牧其中，而无城郭。疑此则春秋之山戎病燕者也。齐桓公束马悬车，涉辟耳之溪，见登山之神，取其戎菽冬葱布于诸侯，盖近之矣。口占一篇因以传疑。”据此知为初至其地时所作。张尚英年谱系此诗于本年（仁宗至元二年）除夕，是未能区分去程与归程。）</span><div id='poem_499156' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499156' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499156?labeling=true' target='_blank'>古北口</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_499156")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_1_499156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_499156'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_499156_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奉使契丹途中过古北口，有《古北口对月》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十二。诗中有不知归期思念亲人之意，又于驿馆见月，而刘敞完成使命重过古北口在除夕，不得见月，可知此诗作于初过古北口北上之时。）</span><div id='poem_498793' id='poem_sentence_2_498793'>他日刀头问，何时客寝安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498793'>因之千里梦，共下白云端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499239'>我持汉节议和亲，北上边关极海滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_499239'>宜有鬼神阴受命，劲风来埽幕南尘。<div 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奉使契丹途中过古北口，游《杨无敌庙》，作《杨无敌庙》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》卷二十八。诗题下自注：“在古北口。”张尚英年谱系此诗于此年（仁宗至和二年）十二月，但十二月已是返程，此诗当作于初至古北口时。）</span><div id='poem_499144' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499144' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499144?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨无敌庙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span 承德

id='poem_sentence_1_498753'>旷原开碛口，别道入松亭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498753'>虏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>马寒随草，奚车夕戴星<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498753'>忽悲田子泰，寂寞向千龄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498753'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498753'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_498753_0'>⑴ 自注：此馆以南属奚，山溪深险。以北属契丹，稍平衍，渐近碛矣。别一道自松亭关入幽州，甚径易。虏（原作敌，据广雅本改）常秘不欲使汉知。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_498753_0'>⑵ 原作敌，据明抄本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十一。诗题下自注：“自檀州东北入山，到铁浆馆出山，凡八程。”可知作于铁浆馆附近。又，所谓檀州入山、铁浆馆出山之“山”，据地形图应是燕山山脉。）</span><div id='poem_498700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498700' class='poemTitle id='poem_title_498700_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_498700_0'>① 自檀州东北入山，到铁浆馆出山，凡八程</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498700'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498700'>万里亘东西，连峰隐朔陲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498700'>今朝识天意，正欲限华夷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498700'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498700_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='88c8467f92f7461ab7fb2cdfdec2892c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("88c8467f92f7461ab7fb2cdfdec2892c");'><span id='88c8467f92f7461ab7fb2cdfdec2892c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，37岁</div><div id='88c8467f92f7461ab7fb2cdfdec2892c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年12月27日</a>　奉使契丹返程，十二月二十七日重经柳河馆，作《柳河》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十八。明抄本题作“十二月二十七日宿柳河，闻永叔是日宿松山，作七言诗寄之。自柳河直路趋松山不过三百里，然虏讳不肯言。汉使常自东道，更白隰长兴，折行西北，屈曲千余里乃与直路合。自此稍西南出古北口矣。”）</span><div id='poem_499146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>柳河<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年12月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_499146")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_499146_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_499146_0'>① 名贤本、明抄本等题作十二月二十七日宿柳河闻永叔是日宿松山作七言寄之自柳河直路趋松山不过三百里然虏讳不肯言汉使常自东道更白隰长兴折行西北屈曲千馀里乃与直路合自此稍西南出古北口矣</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_499146'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_499146'>相望不容三日行，多岐无奈百长亭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_499146'>欲知河柳春来绿，正似山松雪后青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_499146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_499146'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_499146_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
