赤峰
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c5ee3841734b4a11a325ee5e604b879c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c5ee3841734b4a11a325ee5e604b879c");'><span id='c5ee3841734b4a11a325ee5e604b879c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，37岁</div><div id='c5ee3841734b4a11a325ee5e604b879c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奉使契丹，抵达中京，作《过中京走马上平安奏状》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十四。张尚英年谱系此诗于仁宗嘉祐元年正月，是未能判断刘敞归程日期致误。）</span><div id='poem_498883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过中京走马上平安奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498883")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498883'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498883'>载驱冬<span class='inlineComment2'>（名贤本作驱车终）</span>岁极<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>河源<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，状奏今朝款<span class='inlineComment2'>（名贤本作叩）</span>帝阍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498883'>目断白云浮魏阙，心先飞骑向中原。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498883'>揣摩讵试衡人术，感激空衔国士恩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498883'>犹使匈奴戴黄屋，南归惭吊陆公魂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498883'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498883'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_498883_1'>⑴ 原作拯，据名贤本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_498883_2'>⑵ 自注：北廷在横水北，自云（原作云自，据名贤本改）天潢也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498883_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
宿州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='72dbd27b21224b10a943a5ec6df6a336_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("72dbd27b21224b10a943a5ec6df6a336");'><span id='72dbd27b21224b10a943a5ec6df6a336_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，38岁</div><div id='72dbd27b21224b10a943a5ec6df6a336' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　作《宿州道中逢圣俞入京》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_498096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498096?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿州道中逢圣俞入京</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498096")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498096'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498096'>翩翩河中船，一西复一东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498096'>相逢且不留，相别何时逢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498096'>黄鹄安稻粱，有时顾池笼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498096'>一为沧浪去，不复思樊中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498096'>哀君苍发白，扰扰悲途穷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498096'>努力千万乘，寄声谢醉翁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498096'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_498096_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
东平
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='67c0f68123d449b7b2069074d3f47d2a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("67c0f68123d449b7b2069074d3f47d2a");'><span id='67c0f68123d449b7b2069074d3f47d2a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>，40岁</div><div id='67c0f68123d449b7b2069074d3f47d2a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年6月</a>　六月，至郓州，有《郓州谢两府启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十四。）</span><div id='poem_1173705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郓州谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173705")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173705'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173705'>右，某启：四月十六日，蒙恩授起居舍人、知郓州事兼西路安抚使，已于某月日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173705_comment'></div>朝廷之士贵际，而骤陟侍从之严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173705_comment'></div>社稷之守重民，而荐叨屏翰之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173705_comment'></div>智所不及，人其谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173705_comment'></div>盖材各有宜，赏欲无僭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173705_comment'></div>昔寿王东郡，见谴玺书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173705_comment'></div>买臣会稽，许奉计最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173705_comment'></div>或负课自脱，或终更亟还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173705_comment'></div>以彼具绝人之材，犹未免旷位之责，而某方申锡明诏，优游便藩，岂自谓拨烦之宜，殆必有过情之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173705_comment'></div>伏惟某官，衡石多士，股肱本朝，盛德处怀，至公期物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173705_comment'></div>袁丝陋于学，宁有不得居中之嫌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173705_comment'></div>潘岳拙于长，固宜自试用短之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173705_comment'></div>方当上师法令，下勤簿书，庶几乐职之风，仰酬造物之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1173705_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　作《自淮南移东平兼西路安抚使六月五日初入东界得快雨是时齐鲁久旱欣然作小诗示攽奉世等聊志一时意耳》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十九。）</span><div id='poem_499202' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499202' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499202?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自淮南移东<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>平兼西路安抚使六月五日初入东界得快雨是时齐鲁久旱欣然作小诗示攽奉世等聊志一时意耳</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_499202")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_499202_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_499202_0'>① 原作天，据敞自扬州徙知郓州，兼京东西路安抚使，郓州为古东平，据改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_499202'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_499202'>东郊问俗拥征辕，天与为霖破郁烦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_499202'>惭愧泰山云触石，误疑刺史雨随轩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_499202_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_499202'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_499202_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在郓有治绩；作《郓州谒庙文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十。）</span><div id='poem_1173956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郓州谒庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173956")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173956'>维年月日，起居舍人、知制诰、知郓州军州兼劝农群牧使、京东西路按抚使刘某，谨以清酌庶羞，祭于天齐仁圣帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173956_comment'></div>某受朝命，来守兹土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173956_comment'></div>四履之内，山林川泽，苟民所瞻仰者，皆得以礼秩祭，而况岱宗乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173956_comment'></div>故躬执豆笾，进见庙貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173956_comment'></div>神亦昭于厥诚，大庇下民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173956_comment'></div>尚享！</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1173956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　作《郓州祷雨文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十。）</span><div id='poem_1173957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郓州祷雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173957")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173957'>某年月日，某官某，谨以清酌庶羞，祭于东岳天齐仁圣帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173957_comment'></div>某初署政，周询民事，佥曰：春夏闵雨，至于六月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173957_comment'></div>非不雨也，下雨而不甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173957_comment'></div>此乃《春秋》所记，圣人所忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173957_comment'></div>故祗祓厥身，分遣有司，将以吉日丁酉，乞灵于尔大神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173957_comment'></div>未及厥期，而雨三降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173957_comment'></div>岂谓至诚，能昭于天？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173957_comment'></div>惟尔大神，实监其衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173957_comment'></div>曷敢隐神之赐，使人不闻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173957_comment'></div>躬执祀事，以彰灵德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173957_comment'></div>神亦顾哀下民，永终厥惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173957_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1173957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在郓州，造东平乐郊池亭，作《东平乐郊池亭记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十六。）</span><div id='poem_1173882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东平乐郊池亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173882")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173882'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173882'>古者，诸侯虽甚陋，必有苑囿车马钟鼓之好，池台鸟兽鱼鳖之乐，然后乃能为国，非以娱意崇不急也，以合士大夫、交宾客贤者而同吏民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173882_comment'></div>《蟋蟀》、《山枢》、《车邻》、《驷驖》、《有駜》之诗是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173882_comment'></div>不然则觳，觳者墨术也，不侈于礼乐，不晖于度数，曰「人我之养，毕足而止」，亦瘠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173882_comment'></div>夫东平，盖古之建国，又有州牧连率之政，于今为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173882_comment'></div>其地千里，其四封所极，南则梁，东则鲁，北则齐，三者皆大国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173882_comment'></div>其土沃衍，其民乐厚，其君子好礼，其小人趋本，其俗习于周公、仲尼之遗风馀教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173882_comment'></div>可驯以诗书，而不可诡以朱墨，诡以朱墨，鄙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173882_comment'></div>郓故有负城之园，其废盖久，士大夫无所于游，四方之宾客贤者无所于观，吏民无所于乐，殆失《车邻》、《驷驖》、《有駜》之美，而况于《蟋蟀》、《山枢》之陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173882_comment'></div>敞以谓非敦诗书、节礼乐之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173882_comment'></div>据旧造新，筑之凿之，增之扩之，营之辟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173882_comment'></div>有堂有台，有池有榭，有坞有亭，有馆有南北门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173882_comment'></div>堂曰燕誉，台曰陈󶣌，池曰芹藻，榭曰博野，坞曰吾竹，亭曰玩芳，馆曰乐游，南门曰舞咏，北门曰熙春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173882_comment'></div>其制名也，或主于礼，或因于事，或寓于物，或谕于志，合而命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173882_comment'></div>以其地曰乐郊，所以与上下同乐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173882_comment'></div>其草木之籍：松、梧、槐、柏、榆、柳、李、梅、梨、枣、梬、柿、安榴、来檎、木瓜、樱桃、葡萄，太山之竹，汶丘之筱，峄阳之桐，雍门之荻，蒲圃之槚，孔林之香草奇药，同族异名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173882_comment'></div>洛之牡丹，吴之芍药、芙蓉、菱芡、亭兰、菊、荇、茆，可玩而食者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173882_comment'></div>孟子曰：「贤者而后乐此，不贤者虽有此不乐也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173882_comment'></div>吾其敢自谓贤乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173882_comment'></div>抑亦庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173882_comment'></div>后世将必有追数吾过者矣，吾请以此谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1173882_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　在郓州，屡游乐郊，作《乐郊陈渔台下柏林中结茅作小亭命曰幽素本懿臣刑部之书也谢且戏之》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷七。）</span><div id='poem_497935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_497935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/497935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐郊陈渔台下柏林中结茅作小亭命曰幽素本懿臣刑部之书也谢且戏之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_497935")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_497935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_497935'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_497935'>结茅更何好，列柏自成林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_497935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_497935'>素履宜独往，幽人欣宿心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_497935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_497935'>炎辉翳羽盖，清吹和瑶琴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497935'>稍与事物远，忽如丘壑深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497935'>良无山水趣<span class='inlineComment2'>（名贤本作乐）</span>，安得契知音。<div id='poem_sentence_4_497935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_497935'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_497935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　作《郓州乐郊陈渔台下作幽素亭铭其石柱》作品：《郓州乐郊陈鱼台下作幽素亭铭其石柱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十九。）</span><div id='poem_1173900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郓州乐郊陈渔台下作幽素亭铭其石柱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173900")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173900'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173900'>茅为宇，石为柱，幽且素哉，君子之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173900_comment'></div>石为柱，茅为宇，安且固哉，君子之度。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1173900_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　作《九月三日游乐郊作五言赠同游》，梅尧臣有和诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷十三。）</span><div id='poem_498181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498181?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九月三日游乐郊作五言赠同游</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498181")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_498181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498181'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498181'>昔在西省直，常有中园思。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498181'>今来非吾室，犹称宣城诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498181'>芳郊后摇落，秋初尚华滋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498181'>丹宝何纂纂，黄花复离离。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498181'>俯见渊鱼翔，仰观云鸟嬉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_498181'>物性附所适，吾生亦尔期。<div id='poem_sentence_5_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_498181'>置酒得同好，追胜不知疲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_498181'>和歌凉风起，看舞白日移。<div id='poem_sentence_7_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_498181'>兴言想丘壑，弱丧惭旌麾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_498181'>负郭如办此，怀金宁足为。<div id='poem_sentence_9_498181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_498181'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_498181_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　作《自淮南迁东平移后土庙瓊花植于濯缨亭此花天下独一株而永叔为扬州作无双亭以赏之彼人别号八仙花也或云李卫公所赋玉蕊花即此聊以小诗寄其所从来》诗。作品：《自淮南迁东平移后土庙琼花植于濯缨亭此花天下独一株而永叔为扬州作无双亭以赏之彼人别号八仙花也或云李卫公所赋玉蕊花即此聊以小诗寄其所从来》(海内无双玉)<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十九。）</span><div id='poem_499288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>琼花<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序原以序文为题，今据刘本补）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_499288")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_499288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_499288'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_499288'>海内<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>无双玉蕊花，异时来自八仙家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_499288'>鲁人得此天中树，乞与春风赏物华。<div id='poem_sentence_1_499288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_499288'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_499288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_499288'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_499288_0'>⑴ 名贤本、明抄本作淮海</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_499288_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年8月</a>　八月，上《谏仁宗节游观疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1173630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏仁宗节游观疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173630")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173630'>臣闻爱至者虑常过，而忧远者言必深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173630_comment'></div>臣在阙门之外，备东藩之守，诚不当越职出位，以干言责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173630_comment'></div>然窃惟忠臣之义，虽在畎亩，犹不忘君，况如臣者，岂得已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173630_comment'></div>陛下少赐详择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173630_comment'></div>昔周公作《无逸》以戒成王，其言曰：「商王中宗及高宗及祖甲及文王皆以无淫于观、于逸、于游、于田，是以膺无疆之福，子孙蕃昌」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173630_comment'></div>此圣人之至言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173630_comment'></div>陛下临政以来，履而行之三十七年矣，百姓赖陛下之德，养老长幼，人遂其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173630_comment'></div>自三代、汉、唐之盛，未有及于今日者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173630_comment'></div>臣愿陛下日谨一日，与天无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173630_comment'></div>比闻车驾数临苑囿，置酒观乐，虽圣心处之，自有常节，而议者亦谓太频。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173630_comment'></div>臣恐近习苟于承意而不能谏，大臣限以体貌而不得言，如此则传闻四方，未副盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173630_comment'></div>外之则嫌怠于政事，有游观之好；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173630_comment'></div>内之则疑酣于酒德，违摄生之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173630_comment'></div>孔子曰：「乐宴乐，损矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173630_comment'></div>臣愿陛下玩心于神明，养之以清静，职止于中声，毋以烦耳，味止于实气，毋以爽口，则自天祐之，吉无不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173630_comment'></div>孔子曰：「乐节礼乐，益矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173630_comment'></div>惟陛下裁幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1173630_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年10月</a>　十月，诏于景灵宫建郭皇后影殿，刘敞上《论景灵宫不当建郭后影殿疏》作品：《论景灵宫不当建郭皇后影殿疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1173602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论景灵宫不当建郭后影殿疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173602")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173602'>臣所领礼院得御药公文，称奉圣旨，送画到景灵宫广孝殿后，建郭皇后影殿图子一本详定者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173602_comment'></div>其图子已别具状缴奏讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173602_comment'></div>臣伏见近日京师木土之功，靡耗国用，其弊特深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173602_comment'></div>原其本因，只为差内臣监修，利于偷窃官物，及讫功之后，侥求恩赏，以故多起事端，务广兴作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173602_comment'></div>其甚则托以祖宗神御，张皇事势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173602_comment'></div>近年以来，如此兴造，略无虚岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173602_comment'></div>伏以景灵宫建自先朝，以尊奉圣祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173602_comment'></div>陛下又建真宗皇帝、章懿太后神御殿于其间，天下之人皆知陛下奉先广孝之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173602_comment'></div>然则此宫乃陛下奉亲之所，今乃欲以后宫已废未复之后，建殿与先帝太后并列，有渎神灵，莫此之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173602_comment'></div>臣窃谓事决不出于圣意，皆小人私与兴作，有所侥求尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173602_comment'></div>盖自前世，帝王于宗庙之外别为庙享，以追奉祖宗者则有之，未闻有自追奉其妃后者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173602_comment'></div>盖小人不识事体，但茍一时之利，不思损亏圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173602_comment'></div>伏乞特赐寝罢，以全典礼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1173602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　赵概罢翰林侍读学士，将出知郓州，刘敞作《寄东平侍读叔平侍郎》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十九。）</span><div id='poem_499249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_499249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/499249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄东平侍读叔平侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_499249")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_499249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_499249'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_499249'>曲榭层台花木深，春风千骑盛登临。<div id='poem_sentence_0_499249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_499249'>高山流水非无意，正得君来慰我心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_499249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_499249'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_499249_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年12月</a>　到永兴任，上《论孙琳打量均税事奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《续资治通鉴长编》卷一九二。）</span><div id='poem_1173636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论孙琳打量均税事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173636")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173636'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173636'>孙琳在河中府，用方田法打量均税，百姓惊骇，各恐增起税租，因此斫伐桑柘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173636_comment'></div>赖转运使薛向处处张榜告谕，方得暂止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173636_comment'></div>访闻只打量万泉一县，近须一年乃毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173636_comment'></div>蒙减者则必欣喜，被增者自然怨嗟，词诉狱讼，恐自此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173636_comment'></div>乞且召还孙琳，更俟丰岁，庶灾伤之馀，不至惊扰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1173636_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年12月</a>　作《永兴到任谢邻路启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十五。）</span><div id='poem_1173727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永兴到任谢邻路启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173727")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173727'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173727'>右，某启：某过膺朝綍，擢侍经帷，仍委使符，来临雍部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173727_comment'></div>内惟鄙朴之质，私计便安之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173727_comment'></div>就阴寡尤，处远无竞，省技能之至短，顾荣幸之实多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173727_comment'></div>此盖某官，推毂众材，提衡清议，假阳秋之丰润，垂虹蜺之末光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173727_comment'></div>义均同升，爱忘所短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173727_comment'></div>矧复土宇相错，柝声交闻，袭岂弟之风流，聆中和之成颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173727_comment'></div>亦足以祓饰固陋，优游绪馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173727_comment'></div>驰慕之深，启处宁舍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173727_comment'></div>伏冀上为眷倚，精调寝兴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1173727_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　作《永兴到任谢宋承旨启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷四十三。宋祁嘉祐六年三月尚为翰林学士承旨（据《资治通鉴长编》卷六十八），此处宋承旨应即是宋祁。）</span><div id='poem_1173670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永兴到任谢宋承旨启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173670")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173670'>右，某启：肃将命书，临署吏牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173670_comment'></div>藐是空疏之质，寄以会繁之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173670_comment'></div>方地数千，连城累百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173670_comment'></div>内修民社之政，外总兵戎之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173670_comment'></div>僶俛事为，经营分表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173670_comment'></div>力非其任，智不逮心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173670_comment'></div>此盖某官雅怀并容，馀论推假，不遗三益之素，使就一麾之安，顾恐非才，终无云补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173670_comment'></div>冀因德辉之及，犹有期月之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173670_comment'></div>方阻披瞻，曷胜铭向！</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1173670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年12月</a>　王素自成都迁知开封过长安，刘敞作《京尹仲议侍读自成都赴阙将过长安先寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十三。）</span><div id='poem_498835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>京尹仲议侍读自成都赴阙将过长安先寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498835")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498835'>都城一别远相望，楚水秦山各异方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498835'>每颂中和传四子，重闻京兆得三王。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498835'>执经误接金华袐，卧阁惊看鬓色苍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498835'>逃暑肯为千日饮，能无歌舞荐清觞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498835'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　在永兴任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年3月</a>　三月，次子刘奉世中王俊民榜进士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　是年，伯父刘立言卒，有《伯父挽词》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十三。）</span><div id='poem_498809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伯父挽词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_498809")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_498809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498809'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498809'>四十宾兴七十归，清风远与古人稀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498809'>未如彭祖犹为夭，颇似桐乡得所依<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498809'>何路可能奔远日，此生无复待乌衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498809'>故寻庭树丁宁诲，东望吴门涕自挥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498809'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_498809'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_498809_0'>⑴ 自注：大茔在京师，伯父尝为长洲，因遂葬焉。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_498809_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　为张沔作墓志铭。作品：《故朝散大夫尚书刑部郎中致仕上柱国赐紫金鱼袋张公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷五十三。）</span><div id='poem_1173932' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1173932' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1173932?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故朝散大夫尚书刑部郎中致仕上柱国赐紫金鱼袋张公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐六年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(22923, "北宋", "刘敞", "poem_title_1173932")'>刘敞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1173932_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1173932'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1173932'>公讳沔，字楚望，姓张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1173932_comment'></div>其先出留侯子房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1173932_comment'></div>三国之分，纮仕孙氏，由是为江南人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1173932_comment'></div>其后居鄱阳者曰子员，子员生瑶，瑶徙建安之浦城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1173932_comment'></div>瑶生厉，厉生大王父从晟，从晟生曾王父赟，赟生王父霭，霭生皇考瑰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1173932_comment'></div>自王父而上，皆仕南唐，不及见天下之平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1173932_comment'></div>皇考见天下之平，而早世不及仕，故不闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1173932_comment'></div>公之孤，八岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1173932_comment'></div>虽幼，知感慕，沉静不戏狎，异于他儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1173932_comment'></div>少长，发其家书读之，勤志强力，期以文学成名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1173932_comment'></div>当是时，杨文公以文章名一世，于公乡里外姻也，因起从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1173932_comment'></div>游杨氏之门者常数十百人，而公以才见称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1173932_comment'></div>祥符初，举进士甲科，得试校书郎，知抚州临川县，再调睦州遂安县，治皆有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1173932_comment'></div>用荐者言，改大理寺丞、知平阳县，迁殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1173932_comment'></div>母忧去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1173932_comment'></div>服除，知溧水县，转太常博士、通判温州，赐绯衣、银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1173932_comment'></div>庄献称制，张旻以旧德用，骄僭乱法，公上书请出旻补外事，虽不即行，然士大夫忻然向之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1173932_comment'></div>擢御史台推直官，转尚书屯田、都官员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1173932_comment'></div>尝奉使决大狱，朝中称其平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1173932_comment'></div>丞相李文忠公善之，拜侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1173932_comment'></div>数月，吕文靖复入相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1173932_comment'></div>二人者不相能，争于上前，以谓故事三院由中丞荐，不当以执政用，出公知信州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1173932_comment'></div>既至，又移福州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1173932_comment'></div>岁馀，乃复召还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1173932_comment'></div>言事引大体、正得失而已，不茍细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1173932_comment'></div>充开封府判官，转兵部员外郎，改三司盐铁判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1173932_comment'></div>出为淮南转运使，赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1173932_comment'></div>转工部郎中，复入为盐铁判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1173932_comment'></div>假谏议大夫使契丹，还言：敌情慢，疑有非常，宜敕边为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1173932_comment'></div>既而虏果以兵临境，求关南地，如公策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1173932_comment'></div>庆历二年，加直史馆，知陕州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1173932_comment'></div>明年，转刑部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1173932_comment'></div>元昊入泾原，败葛怀敏数十万之师，关中震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1173932_comment'></div>兵少不足自守，朝议不暇远发，使中贵人即崤渑之间，遮四路归戍，悉还补其阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1173932_comment'></div>兵久乘塞，自以得生归与妻子相见，复驱之就死地，人人怨呼，以言相激，拔刃彍弩，且欲绝河桥为变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1173932_comment'></div>中贵人无若之何，疾驰入陕，以诏书属公而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1173932_comment'></div>吏民骇惧奔逃，公单马出城，矫诏谕之曰：「贼已出境，受诏，诸军趣还营，毋得差池」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1173932_comment'></div>众见公之易也，帖然皆敛兵就道，莫复諠哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1173932_comment'></div>于是范文正经略关中，梁丞相奉使延州，皆奏议以公权事合变，消乱止祸，宜厚其赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1173932_comment'></div>朝廷不能用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1173932_comment'></div>契丹复修好，除边关备，徙公河北转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1173932_comment'></div>初，保州以被边故，戍兵廪赐厚他处，及张温之为转运使，议有所增损，军中怨之，相率杀守佐，闭城反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1173932_comment'></div>诸将闻变，争欲急攻城，大兵会城下几十馀万，公独不听曰：「兵骄，故作乱耳，民不反也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1173932_comment'></div>攻城必多所残，百姓何罪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1173932_comment'></div>且城未易攻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1173932_comment'></div>与之相反覆，诸将不能夺，乃登东关门，呼首恶者，谕以祸福，使出降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1173932_comment'></div>众皆踊跃，投兵杖再拜曰：「公活我，愿见诏书，面缚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1173932_comment'></div>后旬馀，天子为遣近臣受其降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1173932_comment'></div>卒全一城者，公本谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1173932_comment'></div>犹以事不先觉，贬秩知汝州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1173932_comment'></div>富丞相宣抚河北，封敕不下，曰：「张某有谋，功乃当赏，奈何夺之位」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1173932_comment'></div>然天子以辈例皆贬，故不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1173932_comment'></div>公为人温恕仁让，在朝廷恂恂无所竞，称为博厚长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1173932_comment'></div>至临急变，勇锐坚决，以身蹈不测，处之不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1173932_comment'></div>其治军旅，应变画策，能任大事，虽宿将无以校得失，百姓赖以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1173932_comment'></div>岂所谓仁者必有勇耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1173932_comment'></div>移知宿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1173932_comment'></div>初，陈恭公有所爱吏，私属公，公不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1173932_comment'></div>及其在位，因事左迁公都官员外郎，监宣州税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1173932_comment'></div>士大夫由此恶之，不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1173932_comment'></div>于其免相也，乃复得工部郎中、知广德军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1173932_comment'></div>又迁刑部郎中、江南东路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1173932_comment'></div>召还，判三司户部勾院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1173932_comment'></div>未几，自请治明州，有诏视三路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1173932_comment'></div>岁满，当入朝，因上章请老于苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1173932_comment'></div>天子许焉，用其少子为州从事，以便奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1173932_comment'></div>初，公以材进，数试繁剧，有异效，世许其任公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1173932_comment'></div>其后失意更不迁，而新进常辈，名位顾多超处其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1173932_comment'></div>自丞相以下，数称其功，理其枉，然遂终不用十有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1173932_comment'></div>他人为公恨，而公处之晏然，未尝寘色辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1173932_comment'></div>性廉，不治家人活业，仰俸禄以生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1173932_comment'></div>而厚于宗族乡党宾客，所资养周给，称其意厚薄，初不计有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1173932_comment'></div>及其归家居也，囊箧无馀赀，所居才蔽风雨，饮食或日阙，亦不以累其志，改其乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1173932_comment'></div>嘉祐五年某月某甲子无疾卒，享年七十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1173932_comment'></div>积阶朝散大夫，勋上柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1173932_comment'></div>夫人魏氏封某县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1173932_comment'></div>子三人，皆孝谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1173932_comment'></div>讽，太子中舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1173932_comment'></div>诜，太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1173932_comment'></div>诲，则州从事者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1173932_comment'></div>女五人，皆嫁名家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1173932_comment'></div>明年某月某日葬某县某乡之穹隆山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1173932_comment'></div>吾闻有阴德者有阳报，不在其身，在其子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1173932_comment'></div>若公之德多矣，殆亦其后且大乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1173932_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1173932'>仕系其逢，进退有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1173932_comment'></div>嗟我张公，长者之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1173932_comment'></div>排难寝兵，洞然至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1173932_comment'></div>不伐不矜，弃功与名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1173932_comment'></div>富贵磨灭，令德则长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1173932_comment'></div>惠之在人，世以不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1173932_comment'></div>穹隆之葬，公则有子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1173932_comment'></div>宜尔子孙，尚食庙祀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_91_1173932_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年4月</a>　四月，迁礼部郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年9月</a>　九月，大飨明堂，进封彭城郡开国侯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年3月</a>　三月辛未，仁宗崩，刘敞作《挽仁宗皇帝歌四首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十二。）</span><div id='poem_498719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>挽仁宗皇帝歌四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_498719'>汉恩隆四世，商历盛三宗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498719'>与子孙能继，宁民户可封。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498719'>云归疑厌代，鼎就莫攀龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_498719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_498719'>庙乐兼韶武，应传盛德容。<div id='poem_sentence_3_498719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498719'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_498719_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_498720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_498720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/498720?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498720'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498720'>措刑文武后，四十有馀年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498720'>几与华胥比，宁知帝力然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_498720'>占龄无协梦，弃躧趣登山。<div id='poem_title_498721_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_498721'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_498721'>不阵威逾远，无为俗自柔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_498721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_498721'>诗书通月窟，箫勺靖炎陬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_498721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_498722_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月</a>　四月，英宗即位，进吏部郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　在永兴任，作诗《病中口占七言奉送前成都尹吕宝臣龙图还朝》送吕公著回朝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《公是集》（文渊阁四库全书本）卷二十五。）</span><div id='poem_498961' -----title
汝州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d1aed8cfe1c44c2d9762079ed4ab7703_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d1aed8cfe1c44c2d9762079ed4ab7703");'><span id='d1aed8cfe1c44c2d9762079ed4ab7703_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1066')">1064-1066年</a>，46-48岁</div><div id='d1aed8cfe1c44c2d9762079ed4ab7703' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年9月</a>　九月，除知卫州，改汝州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年11月</a>　在汝州，十一月，上郊，进封开国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年4月</a>　在汝州，四月，迁右谏议大夫，不久召还阙。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='580ef822a8ba4f6a80e85605f58d1695_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("580ef822a8ba4f6a80e85605f58d1695");'><span id='580ef822a8ba4f6a80e85605f58d1695_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1068')">1067-1068年</a>，49-50岁</div><div id='580ef822a8ba4f6a80e85605f58d1695' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年1月</a>　正月，英宗崩，神宗嗣位，改给事中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年4月8日</a>　四月八日，薨于位，享年五十。<br /></div>
